(London) Yesterday, Zhang Xueliang visited Portsmouth Dockyard. The Commander-in-Chief of the British Navy hosted a tea party at the Admiralty. Zhang visited the aircraft carrier HMS Courageous to observe naval exercises and returned to London in the evening. (10th Reuters Dispatch)

Second Day of National Defense Air Exercises 36

The sound of anti-aircraft guns booms

Bombs fall like rain

(Kanto engulfed in smoke)

(Tokyo) One aircraft that attacked Tokyo last night and whose whereabouts were unknown was found today within the territory of the hypothetical enemy. The engine of this aircraft was damaged, and it was forced to land. The second day of air exercises began at 8:30 this morning. At that time, aircraft attacked Tokyo again, and sirens and alarms sounded all at once. Shortly afterwards, the sound of anti-aircraft guns and machine guns on high rooftops was heard everywhere, announcing the progress of the aerial warfare. Soon, enemy aircraft appeared in the sky above the center of Tokyo, and at the same time, explosions and smoke indicated the locations where bombs had been dropped. (10th Reuters Dispatch)

(Tokyo) Last night, the first day of the Kanto air defense exercises, at 8:17, two enemy aircraft suddenly attacked the sky above the imperial capital from the direction of Miura. Upon receiving the alarm, lights were immediately controlled. The imperial capital suddenly became a dark world. At the same time, the anti-aircraft guns installed everywhere began to fire fiercely from their positions. The enemy aircraft retreated in a panic. They attacked again at 10 p.m. Because of the skillful Japanese air defense tactics, they could not use their skills and gave up bombing empty-handed. Therefore, the results of the first day of the exercises were very good. (10th Dentsu Dispatch)

(Tokyo) On the second day of the air defense exercises in the imperial capital, an enemy fleet with aircraft carriers appeared in the sea west of Ogasawara Island this morning before dawn. Upon receiving this first report, the entire city became very tense. At 8:15, enemy aircraft attacked from north of Mito, and the air battle began. At 9:27, three enemy aircraft flew over the headquarters of the Defense Command, and poison gas bombs rained down. Commander Hayashi and others wore gas masks, and the anti-aircraft machine gun teams all began firing. At 10:20, after fierce fighting, the enemy aircraft were repelled. At 11:19, fifteen enemy aircraft attacked again, and the imperial capital was in a dangerous state. The main buildings on the ground were covered with smoke to confuse the enemy aircraft. At that time, air defense aircraft also took off. As a result, after a fierce attack, the enemy aircraft were completely repelled by 1 p.m. (10th Dentsu Dispatch)

(Tokyo) The military, in view of the good results of the Kanto air defense exercises, will conduct air defense exercises in Kansai next June. The participating areas in Kansai are Osaka Prefecture, Wakayama Prefecture, Nara Prefecture, and Hyogo Prefecture. The other prefectures of Mie, Gifu, and Aichi may also join. (10th Dentsu Dispatch)

Japanese Red Anti-War Squad

Destroys Military Telephones 37

(Tokyo) Today is the second day of the Japanese army's Kanto air defense exercises. The Japanese Imperial Palace has its own power plant to prepare for emergencies. The project was completed on August 8, with a power of 300 kilowatts. The Imperial Palace is also subject to light control. Vice Minister of the Imperial Household Agency Otani is the chief air defense officer in the palace. It is reported that after the Tokyo Garrison Command began the air defense exercises, the Japanese Communist Party simultaneously issued instructions to destroy military defenses during the exercises. From July 21, the telephone lines for air defense have been cut off by the Red Anti-War Squad every day. 500 meters were cut off on July 21, 1,500 meters on July 25, 100 meters on August 1, 1,000 meters on August 2, and 800 meters on August 4, totaling 3,900 meters. Since yesterday, military telephones have often been out of order. The Japanese military police attach great importance to this matter and are said to have begun searching for the perpetrators. (10th Hualian Dispatch)

U.S. "Big Navy" Faction Advocates Active Shipbuilding 38

Japanese Large Submarine to be Completed

U.S. President at Hyde Park today received a lengthy declaration from the Navy League, the strongest supporter of the "Big Navy," predicting that the next Congress will authorize the construction of new ships to bring the U.S. Navy to the maximum extent permitted by the London Treaty. The League ridiculed the claim that the U.S. is accelerating the naval competition between the U.S., Britain, and Japan, saying that even after the current shipbuilding program is completed, Japan will have only seven ships less than permitted by the London Treaty, Britain will have fifty ships less, and the U.S. will have one hundred and twenty-one ships less. The current position of the U.S. will weaken its power to demand the maintenance of the current ratio, and in view of the current world situation, which is already buried with explosives, there is even more need for large-scale shipbuilding. (9th National Telegram)

Yokosuka At the Yokosuka Naval Factory, the large submarine tender "Taigei," which is being built diligently, will be completed and launched at the end of November. Japan's China Policy 39

Internal Government Factions in Opposition

Leadership Wants to Seek Participation in Technical Cooperation

Hardliners Advocate Implementing Original Policy

(Tokyo) The Japanese Ministry of Foreign Affairs is paying close attention to Song Ziwen's actions. Foreign Minister Uchida telegraphed Ambassador Debuchi to investigate the content of the Song-Luo meeting, but no accurate report has been received so far. It is said that opinions within the Japanese government are divided into two types regarding our technical cooperation with the League of Nations, namely, the opinions of the government's leadership, such as Uchida and Araki, and the opinions of the military and foreign affairs hardliners on China. The claims of the two factions are listed below: (A) The government's leadership's China policy: (i) To launch a second Manchurian Incident against China is definitely a foolish move given the current state of Japan's finances and economy. (ii) If we act recklessly regardless of the pros and cons, it will definitely trigger a war between Japan and the world. No matter how excellent Japan's military equipment is, it will definitely not be able to win on the battlefield. (iii) Although Song Ziwen's diplomacy in the United States was successful, his campaign in Europe, according to news received by the military and foreign affairs departments, is that although Britain, France, Italy, and Germany did not accept Japan's protest, the authorities of each country have reportedly proposed to Song Ziwen to persuade China to tolerate Japan's participation in technical cooperation, but Song Ziwen has not indicated acceptance of this proposal. Since the internal situation in European countries is like this, we can still use diplomatic means to participate in cooperation. Therefore, at present, it is still wise not to provoke European countries with military action. (iv) Song Ziwen's background is in the capitalists of Jiangsu and Zhejiang. The capitalists of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, like Japanese capitalists, are tired of war. Therefore, Song Ziwen may not dare to adopt a diplomatic policy of military resistance against Japan after returning to China. Based on the various reasons listed on the left, the Japanese government's leadership wants to adopt a peaceful policy to deal with China, but the young military officers of the military, the young and middle-aged factions of the military system of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, and the civilian fascists advocate using tough measures. The reasons they advocate are listed on the left: (i) The capital power of European and American countries is expanding in China, which is detrimental to Japan's future China policy (the so-called continental policy). (ii) In China, which is currently experiencing extreme financial difficulties, if we do not make China submit at this time, a good opportunity will be lost, and it may be difficult to get such an opportunity again in the future. (iii) At a time when European and American strength is insufficient and we must avoid war, it is an excellent opportunity to eliminate European and American forces in China. Japan should use this opportunity to force peace through war and prevent European and American investment in China. (iv) Even if Japan participates in technical cooperation, the result is still to help China expand its military equipment. We may be able to seek temporary peace at present, but the world situation in three years will definitely be unfavorable to Japan. The young officers of the army oppose the government's policy for the reasons mentioned above and collude with the news section of the Ministry of the Army and various newspapers and news agencies to vigorously promote that Japan will not hesitate to stage a second Manchurian Incident to achieve its established China policy. This is the internal situation of the Japanese government's China policy. (10th Hualian Dispatch)

Discusses Jurisdiction Issues 40

Four Hours of Debate with No Result

(Harbin) The Chinese-Eastern Railway's Russian and "Manchu" directors met yesterday and argued for four hours without any resolution. The only issue they discussed was the limitation of the powers of the Russian Director-General. On this point, the "Manchu" directors argued that all documents should in the future be jointly signed by the Russian Director-General and the "Manchu" Co-Director. The Russian side gave the answer, saying that equal powers presented many obstacles in implementation, but this issue could be considered by a specially formed committee. Current Commentary

The Tokyo Air Defense Exercises • Zi 42

The recent air defense exercises in the Kanto region of Japan, centered on Tokyo, are nothing short of a shadow of World War II. The Japanese warlords are acting like madmen, wanting to be enemies with the countries of the world. Because of the shortcomings of their country's topography, they are easily attacked by enemy aircraft in the event of war. Therefore, they are conducting this large-scale air combat rehearsal to increase the practical experience of their air force generals and soldiers and to train their people. This is also the behavior that a militaristic country should have. However, we, the Chinese people who have suffered from Japanese aerial bombardment and who have nothing to say about air defense to this day, cannot help but increase our terror and emotion upon seeing such a lively performance by a powerful neighboring country.

The Japanese air defense exercises this time adopt two principles. One is to defend by attacking, attacking the enemy's base and destroying its attacking power first. The other is to engage in combat when enemy aircraft fly to Tokyo, destroying the enemy in the air. According to our observations, these two principles inherently contain the nature of inevitable failure for themselves. Today, Japan's imaginary enemies are the United States and Russia. The air force base for the United States to fight against Japan is in Hawaii. Once the war starts, the Hawaiian Air Force will definitely move to the Philippines to meet Japanese aircraft on the sea. At the same time, the United States will inevitably use its large fleet of aircraft carriers to threaten various coastal areas of Japan. It seems impossible for the Japanese air force to attack Hawaii, which is very far away, and the fast-moving American aircraft carriers. Russia has long declared to the world, "Training a flight team like a large swarm of locusts to destroy the cities of the imperialists in a few hours." When the opportunity for Japan and Russia to fight arrives, the Russian air force base in Vladivostok may not be easily approached by Japanese aircraft. This is the uselessness of their first principle. As for wanting to destroy enemy aircraft after they have arrived in the skies above Tokyo, it is even more wishful thinking. May I ask, if enemy aircraft are conducting a planned air raid on Tokyo, would they not be fully equipped to defend against Japanese aircraft attacks? We predict that if the air forces of the United States and Russia can reach the skies above Tokyo, they will definitely use a portion to deal with the Japanese aircraft taking off, while the other portion will be responsible for the bombing work. The Japanese aircraft that take off may be able to destroy some enemy aircraft, but Tokyo's sacrifices will definitely not be reduced as a result. This is the uselessness of their second principle. In short, Japan's susceptibility to being strangled by the air forces of other countries is due to its topography. Japanese warlords should not think about remedying other shortcomings and blindly rely on ordinary air combat principles to defend by attacking. This is not a perfect strategy.

Although, the air defense exercises in Tokyo this time, on the one hand, allow the air force authorities to understand the dangers of Tokyo in the event of air combat and to know what to prevent, and on the other hand, allow its citizens to receive practical training so that they can reduce sacrifices in the event of an enemy air raid. Its role should not be underestimated. We must not take a theatrical attitude from across the sea and call it a spectacle. Furthermore, we should not ignore the lessons for us from this move due to the militarism of the Japanese warlords. Today, the people of our country are in need of this kind of training.

Dutch East Indies

Restricting Imports of Japanese Goods 76

Japanese Businesses Severely Affected

(Tokyo) According to information obtained by the Nanyo Kyokai (South Seas Association), extreme anti-Japanese sentiment has recently arisen in the Dutch East Indies. Traders involved in South Seas relations are very angry because the Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Bureau of Commerce has abandoned its responsibility. When the Dutch East Indies, under the guise of protecting domestic industries, imposed extreme import restrictions on cement imported from Japan, limiting the import volume from 600,000 barrels last year to 300,000 barrels this year,

Related traders had called the attention of the Bureau of Commerce and requested appropriate countermeasures. However, the Bureau of Commerce stated that the Dutch East Indies Governor's restrictions only applied to cement imports and did not affect other commodities. It was said that adopting a tough stance at this time would be unfavorable, and the matter was dropped. Subsequently, the Dutch East Indies Governor implemented general and broad import restrictions, and there was a move to pass the import restriction order through the National Assembly. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs' Bureau of Commerce stood by and watched, without thinking of a way to deal with it. It can only be said that it was a mistake. The Japanese goods most severely affected by the import restrictions are cotton yarn and beer. Cotton yarn imported from Japan accounts for 70% of the total import volume of 18,560,000 guilders. The Nanyo Kyokai does not trust the Ministry of Foreign Affairs. Association Director Iizumi Ryosaburo is rushing there on the Chiyoda Maru to promote trade. (10th DenTsushin Dispatch)

The Second to Last Stop on the Return Trip

Italian Air Fleet Arrives in Lisbon 77

Only One of Twenty-Four Aircraft Lost, Performance Can Be Considered Satisfactory

The Azores Islands Need to Establish an International Airport

▲Reuters, Lisbon, 9th: The Italian air fleet arrived in Lisbon this afternoon, the second-to-last stop on its return trip from America to Italy. Upon arriving in Lisbon, it was escorted by 14 Portuguese aircraft and two destroyers, and thousands of people gathered on the hills, waiting for their arrival, shouting cheers. The first aircraft landed on the river at 2:30 PM (Greenwich time), and by 3:45 PM, all the aircraft had arrived in succession. When General Balbo reviewed the guard of honor, the last three aircraft also arrived, and then flew around the parade ground above the Black Horse Square. All the pilots, in memory of Scagliaglia, who died in a plane crash during takeoff in Horta, may refuse all banquets and entertainment.

▲Havas, Lisbon, 10th: After the Italian Minister of Aviation arrived here, he took a short rest and then summoned reporters in the evening to discuss the flight in detail. Referring to the seaplane that crashed in the Azores, he said that this incident did not detract from the success of the flight. Flying across the Atlantic with 24 aircraft and returning to Lisbon with 23 aircraft, the performance cannot be considered bad. General Balbo also said that Lieutenant Scagliaglia's remains would be transported to Lisbon by an Italian warship. He must wait until the lieutenant's funeral arrangements are completed before he can depart and fly back to Ostia, passing through São Miguel in Portugal, Gibraltar, the Balearic Islands in the Mediterranean Sea, and the Strait of Bonifacio (between Corsica and Sardinia). General Balbo praised the achievements of the French pilots Codos and Rossi, saying that the Italian air fleet members met them in New York. This flight was too risky, and if it were an Italian pilot, he would not have allowed it. When someone asked him about the aviation plan he adopted, Mr. Balbo replied, "In aviation issues, one must have a broad vision and be quick." He also said, "The Azores Islands can be used as an international air traffic station, so there should be facilities for seaplanes to land." However, the convenience of this air traffic should be enjoyed equally by all countries and should not be monopolized by one country. Mr. Balbo meant that the cost of building a seaplane landing base could be negotiated by various countries and shared together. After completion, it should be opened so that all commercial airlines can use it. The main reason for Lieutenant Scagliaglia's accident yesterday was that the Azores Islands did not have seaplane landing facilities. "The Italian air fleet's seaplanes are large and heavy, making it not easy to fly as desired. The Azores Islands should build a port several kilometers long as a base for seaplanes to take off and land," and so on. It is now known that the damage to the front of the crashed seaplane is not significant, and the broken part has been completely repaired.

The US Will Have a New Plan Regarding Currency 79

Short-term Debt Converted into Long-term

Control of Circulation Under Study

▲Kokumin, Washington, 9th: It is currently believed here that rumors that the U.S. government will take action on currency soon are due to the fact that President Roosevelt previously instructed Yale University Professor Rogers and Cornell University Professor Warren to design a plan to convert federal short-term debt into long-term debt, which is about to be completed.

▲Havas, Washington, 9th: The United States wants to establish a policy of controlling currency circulation. Treasury Secretary Woodin is currently studying the necessary conditions before this policy can be established. Mr. Woodin is focusing on economic statistics that indicate rising prices and wants to determine the relationship between rising special prices and the purchasing power of American consumers. President Roosevelt is eager to obtain information on this issue to avoid sudden ups and downs in the economic market that hinder the nation's economic recovery. The prices of raw materials have risen to the level of 1910 to 1914. President Roosevelt is satisfied that the rise in special prices has this result, but the standard of living has not obviously increased. However, the President's hope is not limited to this. He intends to bring the special prices back to the level of the years after the Great War, but he has not mentioned how to achieve this goal.

De Valera Proposes Three Motions to Parliament

Revising the Constitution of Southern Ireland 82

Sever All Relations with the British Crown

Necessary Steps to Declare a Republic

Clash Between Blue Shirts and Authorities Inevitable

▲Reuters, Dublin, 9th: Three motions containing important amendments to the Constitution of the Irish Free State were presented to the Irish Free State Parliament today. One will transfer the functions of the British Crown's representative to the Executive Yuan, one will abolish the British Crown's representative's right to refuse to approve motions, and one will terminate the right to appeal to the Privy Council. If these three motions become law, the result will ultimately be the abolition of the post of Governor-General and the cessation of all contact with the British Crown. If the current organization of Parliament remains unchanged, these motions will inevitably become law within a few months. It is generally felt that this is the first necessary step to declare a republic. It is now expected that Chairman de Valera will order a ban on the Blue Shirts from assembling and marching on Sunday. A clash between the Blue Shirts and the authorities seems inevitable. The severity of the clash will depend on the number of Blue Shirts. According to their leader, General O'Duffy, there may be 30,000 marchers on that day.

Legislators Hurl Abusive Language at Each Other 83

De Valera Hooted for the First Time

▲Reuters, Dublin, 10th: Since entering Parliament in 1927, Southern Ireland's Executive Leader de Valera was hooted for the first time today. After four hours of parliamentary debate on the economic panic and the status of unofficial troops, de Valera intended to stand up and speak, but the sound of "You are destroying the country, you are too weak to deal with any situation" suddenly erupted in the chamber. De Valera was greatly angered and loudly defended himself, but legislators hurled abusive language at each other incessantly. Although the Speaker tried to stop it twice, it was ineffective. The Speaker later declared that if there was any more noise, the meeting would be adjourned immediately, and the chamber was slightly quieter. However, as soon as de Valera made a few remarks, the noise started again. Parliament adjourned at 2:15 PM until September 27th. De Valera was ultimately unable to have the opportunity to explain the government's attitude towards the Blue Shirt march on August 13th.

Radio Image and Sound Transmission 86

Will Soon Be Publicly Exhibited in Berlin

▲Kokumin, Berlin, 9th: The German Radio 50th Anniversary Exhibition will open here in about a week. One of the most interesting parts of the exhibition will be the specially set up radio image transmission section. He Long Retreats to Hunan Province 87

Bandit Areas in All Counties of Western Hubei Completely Recovered

Xu Yuanquan Decides to Convene a Rehabilitation Conference

Hankou Communication: He Long's remnant bandits have suffered heavy losses after repeated suppression by Xu Yuanquan's troops. After the recovery of Wuyang Pass, their strength was even more unsustainable. They gathered the remaining troops at Jiaonu Ping, reorganized them, and retreated to western Hunan. He Long is a native of Sangzhi, and there are still many scattered old troops, making it easy to rally. It is inevitable that he cannot forget this place. From western Hubei to western Hunan, Yuyang Pass is a crucial passage. He Long discovered that there were already heavy troops guarding the area and could not fly over. He also feared attracting the attention of the Hunan Army, so he feigned a retreat to Laifeng to show that he would enter Sichuan Province. However, he suddenly broke out of Yexiong Pass on the 7th and invaded Hunan Province. On the 8th, he concentrated in Longshan, attempting to capture Sangzhi and Yongshun to open up a new base. The bandit drama in western Hubei, which had lasted for seven months, was thus completely swept out of the province. The bandit areas in all counties were thus completely recovered. At the beginning of the suppression, Xu Yuanquan adopted a strategy of encirclement and annihilation, with no intention of harming neighboring areas. After taking office as the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Hunan-Hubei Border Region, the planning became even stricter. Now that the bandits have fled to Hunan, he has specially dispatched elite troops to track and suppress them. At the same time, he telegraphed the Hunan Army to block them at key points. A part of the Hunan Army under Liu Jianxu was originally ordered to be transferred to Xu's command and had already been stationed at designated locations. He Jian, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the Western Route, fearing that the strength was still insufficient, increased the dispatch of two brigades to meet the enemy and coordinate with Xu's troops. These newly dispatched two brigades were also requested to be commanded by Xu Yuanquan nearby. It is heard that the actual strength of He's bandits is no more than 3,000 people, and many of the lower-level cadres have disintegrated. It is expected that with the encirclement of the Hunan and Hubei armies, their demise can be expected soon. Xu Yuanquan was supervising the troops on the front line in Changyang a few days ago and returned to Yichang on the 9th. In addition to ordering the troops to continue their efforts to eliminate the remnant bandits, he also paid special attention to the issue of rehabilitation. It is heard that he has decided to convene a rehabilitation conference in Yichang in the near future, inviting county magistrates and local gentry from the counties in the Hunan-Hubei border region to discuss the details of the process. It is found that the counties of Shimen, Cili, Dayong, and Sangzhi in western Hunan, and Hefeng, Wufeng, Laifeng, Xuanen, Enshi, Changyang, and Badong in western Hubei have been ravaged by the bandits for five years. In the last two years, they have been entirely in western Hubei, occupying it three times in total. This time, they have occupied it for more than half a year, and the damage to the local area and the suffering of the people are far beyond what the counties in western Hunan can compare. How to rehabilitate is particularly important. Chairman Chiang has recently telegraphed the Hubei Provincial Government and the Security Department to be responsible for the preparations. The original telegram is as follows: "It is found that the counties of Shihe in western Hubei have been suppressed by Commander-in-Chief Xu leading troops, and bandit nests in various places have been recovered one after another. All matters concerning disaster relief in bandit areas, attracting refugees, organizing Baojia, restoring rural areas, and Qingxiang (cleansing the countryside) should be planned and implemented step by step by the Provincial Government and the Security Department to pacify the area and eliminate bandit troubles." (9th)

Bandit Atmosphere in the Border Area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui Disappears 88

West District Bandit Gang Has Been Defeated

Anqing Communication: Liu Zhenhua, the Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression in the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, has recently been stationed in Huangchuan to supervise the suppression of bandit gangs. He was also serving as the Chairman of Anhui Province, and the position is temporarily held by the Director of the Department of Civil Affairs, Ma Lingfu. It has been two months since Liu went to Huangchuan. Regarding the true situation of bandit suppression, Liang Haiting, a counselor from the headquarters, arrived in the province from Huangchuan and had some discussions with the provincial government. According to him, the situation of bandit suppression in the border area was very detailed. He briefly said that the border area of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui includes the counties of Shangcheng, Gushi, and Huangchuan in Henan, Macheng and Huangzhou in Hubei, and Luan and Lihuang in Anhui. Each of these counties has long been an area occupied by bandits, and years of suppression have not eliminated them. Chairman Chiang then designated it as a bandit suppression area in the border area, giving Liu the special responsibility for handling it. After Liu arrived in Huangchuan, he arranged the suppression troops in a general way, and then accompanied Liu Maoen of the 11th Route Army and moved to the front line in Xiji. The four divisions of Liang Guanying, Hao Mengling, Peng Zhenshan, and the 64th Division (with Liu Zhenhua concurrently serving as the division commander) were the suppression troops, and the rest of the troops were the blocking troops. The general attack began on the 17th of last month. The 64th Division advanced south from Xiji, Liang Guanying's troops advanced east from Xuanhuadian in Luoshan, and Peng Zhenshan's troops advanced north from Huang'an to Tuanshugang. The pursuit troops engaged in fierce battles with the bandits. As a result, the 64th Division successively occupied Shuangshanmen, Wujiawan, Taipingzhai, Wangjiadawo, and other places, Liang's troops occupied Guojiahe, Guanyinshan, and other places, and Peng's troops occupied Taergang, Jianchanghe, and other places. Since then, the three-way pursuit, each division has completely achieved contact, and the road from Huang'an to Jingfujiugeng is unimpeded. At this moment, the bandits in the west district have been completely defeated. In order to prevent their resurgence, Liu specially ordered the 64th Division and the three divisions of Peng, Liang, etc. to be stationed in various places in the west district for strict search and suppression, and ordered the counties in the special district to organize armed civilians to move to the recovered area and plan to restore the countryside. At the same time, he ordered the troops to advance to the east district, and the military affairs are expected to end soon. Liu also prepared a rehabilitation plan and submitted it to Chairman Chiang for review and implementation. The content is to request an appropriation of 4.9 million yuan, with 1 million yuan for the relief of refugees and the remaining 3.9 million yuan for the needs of rural revival. Chiang has agreed to allocate funds for the relief of refugees in the headquarters. As for the funds for rural revival, it is planned to issue rehabilitation public bonds in the three provinces' border area. This level of handling is more difficult and is still under deliberation. What is currently being carried out is to take in refugees from the bandit area and provide immediate relief. At the same time, the armed immigration policy is used to prepare to organize 20,000 people from the militia in the border area, giving each person a gun, plus three bare-handed people, who will go with them, and 80,000 people can be obtained. They are opened into the bandit area, and those with guns are responsible for defense, and the bare-handed people are incorporated into the newly moved people in the bandit area. Funds are currently being raised and actively carried out. (August 9th)

Henan Troops Arrive at Zhu Town and Come into Contact with Bandits

Zhengyang Pass Reinforces Defense, Local Area is Peaceful

Steep Drop in Yellow River Water Level in Shandong Province 90

丨But the Changyuan County, Hebei Province, breached丨

Jinan Correspondence: The Yellow River in Shandong Province has been in a serious situation since the beginning of the rainy season this year, unlike previous years. After receiving the report, the provincial government urgently ordered Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Affairs Bureau, to go to the dangerous engineering sites in the upper reaches to supervise the defense and repair efforts. He was also ordered to report the water situation in the three reaches three times a day. After receiving the order, Mr. Zhang rushed to the upper reaches at noon on the 5th to supervise everything. After three days, all dangerous works were successively repaired and stabilized. Mr. Zhang went to inspect the Shilipu area yesterday (the 7th). It is reported that today (the 8th) he will go to the junction of Hebei and Shandong provinces to inspect the river water situation. Since the breach in Changyuan County, Hebei Province, the water level in Shandong Province has dropped sharply since yesterday (the 7th). Today (the 8th), heavy rain poured down from about 3:00 AM to about 3:00 PM, but the Yellow River water level still dropped significantly. The water level at Luokou dropped 5.8 inches yesterday, and the water level has dropped from over 33.3 meters to 29.7 meters. The dangerous period may be over. (8th)

Results of the Investigation into the Gold Digging Case in Wuchang 91

Report by the Investigation Committee on the Investigation Process

Hankou Correspondence: The case of Peng's theft of gold buried in the Kong residence in Wuchang has been under investigation by a committee organized by the garrison headquarters. After a month and eleven meetings, the committee has now concluded its investigation. Peng Younan, the main culprit in the theft, has been released on bail. On the 9th, a report on the investigation process and handling suggestions will be submitted to the garrison headquarters. This case will soon be finalized. The original report is divided into four parts: ㈠ The process of continuing the investigation. In addition to reporting the situation of each meeting in a timely manner, Zheng Rongtai, the owner of the cement project at the Peng residence, and Zheng Chouya, the shop owner, were summoned to the meeting. Their statements were consistent with those of the worker Tao Shaolian (Tao's statement has been reported earlier). Subsequently, both parties involved were summoned to supplement the facts. Peng Younan was placed under the guarantee of a reliable shop, and Kong Wenxuan was requested to hand over 385 silver ingots and 72 pieces of loose silver of various sizes for safekeeping, as originally agreed. Zheng Rongtai was still ordered to quickly hand over the fugitive excavator Li Changhe for thorough investigation. ㈡ Determination of the case. The site of the buried gold was confirmed to be within Kong Wenxuan's land after on-site inspection. According to Li Changhe and Tao Shaolian, the discovery was made when Li was excavating the Peng family's foundation wall adjacent to the Kong family's wall. Li was a worker for the Peng family and had no reason to excavate the Kong family's wall. Peng Younan's continued excavation had even less legal basis. Moreover, after the discovery, Peng drove away all irrelevant personnel and continued to excavate, which is even more suspected of theft. As for the stolen goods and their quantity, it is difficult to investigate. However, the area of the gold-filled site has been measured, and the volume of the second discovery can also be compared. Furthermore, Li testified that there were yellow strips and large "Ta Ta" (a unit of weight) in the site, which indicates that it was not purely small silver. ㈢ Opinions on Peng Younan's defense statement. 1. Peng stated that the location of the buried gold was not within Kong Wenxuan's land. However, the Kong and Peng walls are close together, making it impossible to hide so much gold. The gold-filled site is indeed in the Kong residence, and the silver excavated for the second time was also in a corner of the site, which was witnessed by everyone. 2. Peng stated that the wall was collapsing and not excavated by him, which is refuted by the testimonies of Li and Tao. 3. Peng stated that Li's testimony did not mention gold, but Li mentioned yellow strips, etc. Although it cannot be concluded that the yellow strips were gold, who can say for sure that they were not gold? ㈣ The opinions of all committee members on the handling of this case. Based on the above points, Peng Younan is considered to be highly suspicious. Now that he has been released on bail, other measures should not be considered. However, whether the excavated material is pure silver or mixed with gold, and what the quantity is, in addition to strictly urging the guarantor Zheng Rongtai to hand over Li Changhe for interrogation, it is requested that a person skilled in surveying and calculation be hired to compare the area of the original gold-filled site with the number of silver ingots discovered the second time, and their volume. If it is assumed that the entire gold-filled site is silver, an accurate calculation should be made, so as to strictly pursue the confiscation of the entire amount for local public welfare undertakings. Kong Wenxuan should also be ordered to hand over the silver discovered the second time in its entirety, so as to fulfill his high-mindedness of disregarding money. (9th)

Smuggling Case at Jiaozhou Customs 92

Forged Documents Used to Extract 1,500 Bags of White Sugar

Two Customs Officers Fled After the Incident

Qingdao Correspondence: Jiaozhou Customs has close cooperative relationship with the Port Authority of this city, and its procedures are strict. Therefore, cases of tax evasion and smuggling are rare. Unexpectedly, a major smuggling case was recently discovered where customs officers colluded with a customs broker to forge documents and illegally extract 1,500 bags of white sugar. After this case occurred, the parties involved were reluctant to announce the facts, so the truth could not be ascertained. It is said that two customs officers on duty that day fled after the incident. The evaded customs duties on the 1,500 bags of white sugar are worth about 9,000 yuan, which is a significant loss for the customs. The discovery of the tax evasion occurred roughly as follows:

On July 25th, when the calculation section of the Port Authority was sorting out the cargo request forms for the 17th of this month, it was suddenly discovered that there were two forms, numbers 575 and 576, requesting a total of 1,500 bags of white sugar. The numbers were repeated, and after checking the customs-stamped delivery slips, there were no items of white sugar extraction. After a detailed investigation, it was discovered that the customs broker had forged the name stamp of Li Xingyan, an employee of the calculation section, and bypassed the calculation section that checks the customs delivery slips. They calculated the wharfage fees themselves, paid the full amount at the collection office, and transported the white sugar out of the customs at about 5:00 PM that afternoon in 125 large carts. After the incident was discovered, in addition to strictly investigating whether any employees of the bureau were involved in the smuggling, the situation was reported to the customs for strict investigation. It has now been found that two customs officers on duty at 6:00 PM that afternoon went to work at 5:00 PM and used clever words to dismiss the previous shift's customs officers. They then secretly released the goods at this time. It is now reported that the customs officers have fled, so the customs is waiting to notify the Public Security Bureau to investigate the people involved in this case. If it is found in the future that employees of the bureau are involved in the smuggling, they will be punished according to the law. (August 7th)

Rampant Bandits in Jiaodong 93

Jiaosha Bus Robbed

Jiaoxian United Association Surrounded

Qingdao Correspondence: The counties in Jiaodong have been ravaged by bandits for years, and the suffering is unspeakable. Fortunately, each county has established a United Village Association, which owns firearms and hires strong men, who are trained during slack farming seasons to provide protection. The bandits have been slightly restrained. Since last year, when Han Fuqu, the chairman of Shandong Provincial Government, ordered the dissolution of all United Village Associations in the counties, the people have no armed forces, and bandits in various places have taken the opportunity to emerge. Kidnappings are heard every day. Now that the green gauze tents of summer have risen, the bandit forces are even more rampant, daring to openly confront the government army and even intercept Jiaosha buses, kidnapping no less than a hundred people, which is truly shocking. The recent bandit situation in Jiaodong is recorded as follows:

(Jiaosha Bus Robbed) At Beidu, where Jiaoxian and Pingdu are adjacent, the terrain is low-lying and covers more than ten acres. It is an area where bandits often appear. This summer, a large group of bandits, numbering about a hundred, with more than eighty Mauser pistols, wearing various colored clothes, and speaking local accents, has been discovered there. They are entrenched there and plundering in all directions. At the end of last month, two Jiaosha buses from Shahe to Jiaoxian were intercepted and surrounded by bandits near the area. They fired their guns as a warning and kidnapped more than thirty passengers. They also forced the two bus drivers to drive the buses to transport goods. After arriving at their destination, they interrogated the hostages one by one, asking about their family property, in order to bargain for ransom. According to those who escaped, the bandits have kidnapped no less than a hundred people before and after. Moreover, since robbing the buses, they have been using the buses to kidnap people. A few days ago, they kidnapped the father of the town chief of Longxing Town and three neighbors.

Page 10

The bus drivers are said to have escaped in the meantime and reported the case to the Jiaoxian County Government. Upon receiving the report, County Magistrate Zhou Lisheng considered the case to be serious and went to the headquarters of the 86th Brigade stationed in Jiaozhou to consult with Brigade Commander Chen Dejian. Brigade Commander Chen immediately dispatched troops to join forces with the militia and the Public Security Bureau to encircle and suppress the bandits. Upon hearing the news, the bandits fled into Pingdu. The troops are currently still tracking them.

(Openly Confronting the Government Army) The bandits at the junction of Pingdu and Jiaozhou have not yet been suppressed, and another group of bandits, numbering about eighty, with fifty or sixty guns, has been discovered in the Qiaoge Zhuang and Zhang Zhuang areas at the junction of Jiaozhou. Upon receiving the report, Gong Zhipu, the head of the third district of Jiaoxian County, reported the case to the county government and requested that troops be dispatched to suppress the bandits. At the same time, he joined forces with the United Village Association of the district to encircle the bandits. On the 2nd of this month, they came into contact with the bandits and engaged in a fierce battle for several hours. Due to being outnumbered, seven members of the association were killed by the bandits. County Magistrate Zhou Lisheng has now accompanied Regiment Commander Zhang of the 86th Brigade, leading a battalion of infantry and several mortars, and is heading to the scene of the incident in armored vehicles to suppress the bandits. They disembarked at Lancun Railway Station and transferred to the scene of the incident to pursue the bandits. It is now reported that the bandits are entrenched in the Zhang Zhuang and Jiajia Lou areas, and sentries have been set up outside the villages, openly confronting the government army. The troops led by County Magistrate Zhou and others arrived in Xiaobu yesterday, only a few miles away from the bandits. They are now seeking an opportunity to advance and suppress the bandits. (August 4th)

Resolution of the Bingtian (Soldier's Land) Case of Tonghai Kenmu (Reclamation and Animal Husbandry) Company 94

(The Executive Yuan Resolved to Waive Compensation)

Tonghai Kenmu Company was founded by Mr. Zhang Jian. Mr. Zhang worked hard, fighting against the tides for thirty years, finally transforming barren saline land into fertile soil and providing a livelihood for tens of thousands of people. When the company was established, the Su and Lang camps had 400 qing of bingtian. In the fourth year of Daoguang of the Former Qing Dynasty, it was decided that Zhang Nanting and Lu Yuhe would permanently lease the land, exert their efforts to enclose and reclaim it. By the twenty-seventh year of Guangxu, after eighty or ninety years, only 160 qing had been reclaimed. The Su camp had only collected rent on 99 qing and some odd acres, and the Lang camp had only collected rent on 61 qing and some odd acres. The remaining 239 qing and some odd acres were all low-lying mud flats that were most difficult to enclose. Only a portion was enclosed by the Zhang and Lu family tenants, which cost a lot of labor. However, the two hurricane tides in the twenty-eighth and thirty-first years of Guangxu washed away the dikes that had been built, as if they had not been enclosed. The seawater was extremely salty. Once it flooded in, even the reclaimed land would immediately turn into saline soil. The tenants were unable to repair it and were willing to include the two washed-down embankments and the unreclaimed mud flats into the company's management. The company would return more than 73,000 yuan in silver to the tenants as compensation for the tenant rights and labor costs. The unreclaimed wasteland was subscribed for shares by converting the silver taels paid by the two towns into standard taels for shares, with each share being 100 standard taels of silver. The Su camp was converted into 44 shares and the Lang camp into 8 shares. At that time, the two towns sent personnel to conduct on-site surveys, and the land was priced for shares. It was reported to the Former Qing Governor of Jiang and approved. After the founding of the Republic of China, the company also registered the land and paid taxes in accordance with regulations. It was also ordered by the Jiangxu Military Governor to transfer the shares of the two camps to the Qingjiang Congee Factory and the Poor People's Factory. The company was instructed to change the names of the account holders. In the seventeenth year of the Republic of China, the Ministry of Finance of the National Government issued a license to ensure credibility. However, some people coveted the high price of the land and concealed the hardships of the initial undertaking. They fabricated facts and initially filed a complaint with the Ministry of Finance, which was not approved. They then accused the company of bribing officials and insulting revolutionary officials, as seen in official documents. At the same time, they reported to the Ministry of Military Affairs that the company was encroaching on military property. After investigating and finding that it was untrue, the Ministry formulated five measures and presented them to the Executive Yuan, ordering the company to pay compensation for the land at the current price. The company believed that this was a private rights dispute and should be under the jurisdiction of the judiciary. It presented the case to the Supreme Court, which decided in August of the twentieth year that the case should be adjudicated by the Haimen County Government in accordance with the law. The Haimen County Government then ruled that the bingtian in question belonged to the company. Even according to the measures formulated by the Ministry of Military Affairs, the fifth item stated that the subscription of shares with the price paid by the two camps was not comparable to encroachment. The Executive Yuan instructed the Ministry of Military Affairs that the ownership of the bingtian reclaimed by the Tonghai Kenmu Company was not denied. The company's ownership of the bingtian was confirmed, and the former Qing and Republic of China governments all recognized it as correct. However, the original plaintiff accused the company of bribing its way through the process and defaming the dignity of the judiciary, as seen in official documents. It was found that the Su and Lang camps still had 160 qing and some odd acres. In the sixth year of the Republic of China, the General Bureau of Official Land in Taiwan estimated the value of the land and transferred it to the people at a price of 1.5 yuan per mu. In the seventeenth year, the Ministry of Military Affairs ordered these transferees to register in accordance with regulations and pay a handling fee of 3 cents per mu, without ordering them to pay the price again. However, the bingtian subscribed for shares was originally barren land. The combined value of the shares and the cost of recovering the tenant rights was more than 3 yuan per mu. Therefore, the company was not suspected of taking advantage of low prices. The company's entire reclaimed land, in addition to being used for public welfare funds, was completely distributed to the shareholders in the fourth and fourteenth years of the Republic of China. Since then, it has been sold and resold, and the ownership has changed hands many times. A small number of shareholders entrusted the company to manage the land on their behalf. The company was only responsible for partial agency responsibilities and had no right to control it under the law. Therefore, based on legal principles, the company had no reason to pay compensation, and it was impossible to pay compensation in fact. However, the original plaintiff still refused to give up the lawsuit. The case was suspended for four years, resulting in a stalemate. If the government were to enforce the compensation, the company would be on the verge of collapse, and the complete rural community would be destroyed. Mr. Zhang Xiaoruo has not been involved in the company's affairs in recent years due to the compilation of his ancestor Mr. Zhang Jian's biography. Seeing that the company was facing false accusations and was in danger of being destroyed, and that the company was the business painstakingly operated by his ancestor, and that the outcome of the case was related to his ancestor's lifelong reputation and the credibility of the entire Nantong business, he had to personally take charge. Based on the above legal principles and facts, he requested the Executive Yuan to withdraw the order for compensation. He also requested the Ministries of Military Affairs and Industry to give preferential consideration and forward the request to the Executive Yuan to withdraw the order for compensation in accordance with the law and the situation. Therefore, the Ministry of Industry's report to the Executive Yuan and the communication to the Ministry of Military Affairs cited Articles 91 and 92, Paragraph 2 of the current Company Law, stating that the case was far back in the Former Qing Dynasty, and the procedures for handling shares with property as capital were not exactly the same. However, the case was approved by the Former Qing Governor of Jiang and a license was issued by the Ministry of Finance of the National Government. Therefore, by comparing it with the current laws and regulations, it could be regarded as having gone through legal procedures and should be considered appropriate. No further compensation should be paid. The Ministry of Military Affairs also stated in its final reply to the Executive Yuan that it respectfully requested the Executive Yuan to review and instruct how to handle the case. After receiving the reports from the two ministries and the company, the Executive Yuan ordered the Ministries of Military Affairs and Industry to jointly review the case. During the review, Deng, a counselor of the Yuan, attended the meeting. Chen, the acting minister of the Ministry of Military Affairs, and Duanmu, the director of the department, attended the meeting. Pi, the section chief of the Ministry of Industry, attended the meeting. The representative of the Ministry of Military Affairs stated that there were no prejudices. The conclusion was then signed and submitted to the President of the Yuan and submitted to the 119th meeting of the Executive Yuan on August 8, which decided to waive the compensation. President Wang and others, in the spirit of democratic governance, believed that if the statutory property rights that had been established for a long time were not protected, the property rights of all citizens would be fundamentally shaken, and the social organization would be destroyed. It was not just a matter of the collapse of a rural community, so they had to protect it and withdraw the order for compensation. The long-pending bingtian case of the Kenmu Company was finally resolved.

Three Ships of the Bohai Fleet Incorporated into the Guangdong Sea Fleet 95

Directly Under the Command of the First Army Group Headquarters

Guangzhou Correspondence: After the three ships of the Bohai Fleet, Haiqi, Haichen, and Zhahe, were transferred to Guangdong, they were incorporated by the Southwest and handed over to the commander-in-chief of the First Army Group for proper organization. Chen Jitang initially planned to subordinate the three ships to the original Japanese Naval Headquarters. In the end, considering that the three ships were coastal defense ships and should not be under the same department as the Jiangfang (river defense) fleet of Guangdong Province, the three ships were incorporated into the Guangdong Sea Fleet. They would be under the command of the commander-in-chief of the First Army Group and not subject to the naval headquarters under the original Japanese Headquarters. After several consultations, it was decided to designate the three ships Haiqi, etc., as the "Guangdong Sea Fleet of the First Army Group of the National Revolutionary Army." Jiang Xiyuan was appointed as the Major General Commander of the Guangdong Sea Fleet in the name of the commander-in-chief of the First Army Group. Ran Hongpian was appointed as the Captain of the Haiqi ship with the rank of Colonel, Tang Jing as the Deputy Captain with the rank of Lieutenant Colonel, Guan Jizhou as the Captain of the Haichen ship with the rank of Colonel, Zhang Fengren as the Deputy Captain with the rank of Lieutenant Colonel, Yang Chaolun as the Captain of the Zhahe ship with the rank of Colonel, Li Baolin as the Deputy Captain with the rank of Lieutenant Colonel, and Zhao Zonghan as the Colonel Chief Instructor of the Guangdong Sea Fleet. The appointment letters for the above officers were brought back to Huangpu by Guan Jizhou, the Captain of the Haichen ship, at 8:00 AM on July 30 and announced to all officers and soldiers on the ship. It is reported that all officers and soldiers of the three ships will not be changed, only the Captains and Deputy Captains will be newly appointed. As for the headquarters of the Guangdong Sea Fleet, its organization is not much different from that of an ordinary fleet headquarters. In addition to the Chief of Staff, there are eight departments under the Commander: Military Supply, Ordnance, Military Medicine, Military Balance, Staff, Adjutant, Secretary, and Engineering. The position of Chief of Staff of the Guangdong Sea Fleet Headquarters has been appointed to Lu Tongyang. Mr. Lu is currently ill and has not yet reported for duty and the position is temporarily held concurrently by the Chief Instructor Zhao Zonghan. The candidates for the heads of each department have also been decided by Jiang Xiyuan, the Commander of the Guangdong Sea Fleet, and submitted to the Commander-in-Chief of the First Army Group for review and approval. Once approved, they will take office separately. The Guangdong Sea Fleet Headquarters is expected to be established this month. The headquarters will be located in Guangzhou, and the three ships will still be docked in Huangpu to consolidate the coastal defense. The total expenses have been greatly reduced and are expected to be over 90,000 yuan per month. (August 1st)

Wuxi Silk Industry Requests Reduction of Freight Rates for Factory Silk 100

Wuxi is the richest silk-producing area in Jiangsu Province. In the most prosperous period of production, it produced more than 40,000 pieces per year. Recently, the silk market has been bleak, and production has also decreased. Previously, when exporting silk, it was always transported by train, and railway freight was also a large source of income. In recent years, freight transport between Wuxi and Shanghai has been fiercely competitive, and many factory silks have been switched to boat transport. Recently, the Railway Bureau is reducing prices to develop freight transport. Twenty or more factories, including Yongtai Dingchang Qiansheng, have jointly written to the Two-Route Administration and the Jinghu Route Traffic Department, requesting a reduction in freight rates for factory silk, in order to ensure that it is still transported by train. The reasons they cited are as follows: ㈠ The silk industry has been failing for years, and the government is trying to provide relief. The freight should still be charged at 2.7 yuan per piece, as before. ㈡ When silk prices were at their highest, each dan (a unit of weight) cost 1,700 or even 2,000 taels. Now that the tael has been abolished and replaced by the yuan, each dan has dropped to 700 or 800 yuan, and freight rates should be reduced accordingly. ㈢ Water transport between Shanghai and Wuxi is very convenient. Freight boats compete to reduce freight rates in order to attract customers, and they also offer various conveniences to shippers, such as deadlines for delivery. The Railway Bureau has sent personnel to investigate the silk transport volume over the years and the current situation in order to submit the findings to the traffic meeting for joint discussion.

Resolution of the Rickshaw Fare Issue 102

The strike of rickshaw pullers in this county, after careful handling by the county government, ended with a full resumption of work on the 8th. The evening before, the Rickshaw Trade Association held its sixth preparatory meeting, following orders to prepare for re-election. The current preparatory committee members submitted a collective resignation to the County Party Headquarters, and it was resolved to send Yao Ganshi to the county government to discuss the rickshaw fare issue. At the same time, a report on the re-election process of the association will be submitted to the County Party Headquarters, the County Government, and the County Chamber of Commerce for record. Yesterday (the 10th), at around 9:00 AM, the county government invited representatives from the Party, government, commerce, and relevant parties to the county for discussions. Those present included County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, Xu Yongji from the County Party Headquarters, Qian Sunqing from the County Chamber of Commerce, Chen Zhandong from the County Property Department, Zhang Fulun from the Technical Office, Ji Zhongliang from the First District Office (representing Qian Xie Zeng), Yao Ganshi and Ren Shuying representing the Rickshaw Trade Association, and Shen Zaichuan and Yi Jingting representing the Yancheng Association, totaling ten people. First, County Magistrate Yan delivered a speech outlining the purpose of inviting the representatives to the government for discussions. Next, Yao Ganshi, representing the Rickshaw Trade Association, spoke about the difficulties faced by the rickshaw industry. He stated that the cost per rickshaw was eleven yuan per month. The previously set fare of 3.7 cents could still cover costs, but it was not implemented due to inconsistent rickshaw prices among businesses. This time, the restoration of the fixed price led to the rickshaw pullers' strike, resulting in significant losses and damaged rickshaws. He requested that the government severely punish the instigators who had been arrested. Then, Shen Zaichuan, representing the rickshaw pullers, stood up and spoke about the difficulties faced by the rickshaw pullers in making a living. He requested that the investors show understanding and reduce the rickshaw fare to maintain their livelihood. He also requested that the maximum rickshaw fare be set at 850 copper coins per rickshaw, and asked the government to leniently punish the rickshaw pullers. Finally, Qian Sunqing, representing the County Chamber of Commerce, expressed his views. Regarding the disputes between the rickshaw industry and the rickshaw pullers, he stated that the rickshaw industry should not stubbornly adhere to its views, and the rickshaw pullers should not be overly insistent. He pointed out that the rickshaws in Wuxi were inferior to those in other counties, with only 70% still usable, and the remaining 30% being dilapidated and difficult to pull. He requested that the authorities take action to address this. He stated that he was in a mediating position, and according to the cause of the case, which was due to administrative actions, he hoped that both sides would respect the county magistrate's intentions and persuade the industry to resolve the issue. The county magistrate did not favor either side and handled the matter impartially. After three hours of discussion, County Magistrate Yan summarized the opinions of all parties and decided on two points regarding the rickshaw fare standard: (1) For rickshaws in good condition, the maximum rental price would be 1,000 copper coins per day per rickshaw. (2) For dilapidated rickshaws, the minimum standard would be 850 copper coins. It was decided that the county government would issue a public notice on the 16th of this month for everyone to comply with. As for the dilapidated rickshaws, the Technical Office would immediately dispatch personnel to inspect each rickshaw company, and those that were too dilapidated would be banned, while those in good condition would be marked for rectification. The meeting adjourned at half-past noon.

Murder Case Occurs Near Tangqiao in Changzhou 103

Chen Jinpei, a villager from Fangqian Village near Tangqiao Town in the Fifth District of Wuyi County, had been rumored for days to have been murdered and his body destroyed to cover up the crime. The nearby Sixth Public Security Bureau and the County Court Procuratorate both sent personnel to investigate. On the 9th, the deceased's mother-in-law, Zhang Chen, and night watchman Wang Liansheng testified at the County Court, providing details about the murder. Subsequently, the County Court received a phone report from the Sixth Public Security Bureau stating that a body, hacked into multiple pieces, had suddenly surfaced in the Xinqiaotou River. Chief Prosecutor Yang Kong dispatched officials to Henglin by car, then hired a boat to proceed. Upon arriving at the crab weir near Xinqiaotou, they saw a foot floating and, after retrieving it, took it to a nearby corpse field. They found that the body had been hacked into nine pieces: one head, two hands, one foot, one lower abdomen, two thighs, and two buttocks. The body was not completely pieced together, missing parts such as the thighs. Everyone who witnessed this tragic scene was deeply saddened. Chief Prosecutor Yang also ordered the forensic officer to examine the deceased's head and found injuries from wooden objects and knife wounds on the back of the head. The corpse's relatives identified it as Chen Jinpei's body without a doubt. The Chief Prosecutor immediately ordered a thorough investigation and instructed the corpse's relatives to prepare a coffin for burial. Chief Prosecutor Yang and others returned to the city, arriving at around 11:00 PM.

Lovers in Zhenjiang Embrace and Jump into the River 104

A man surnamed Jin, a resident of Majia Lane in this port city, works in a certain agency. His son, Jin Wanhua, is 19 years old and studies at a certain school, not yet graduated. He is quite reserved and academically successful. Gao Yue'e, a 17-year-old girl from Jiangdu, who lives with relatives, is in the same class as Jin. Over time, they fell in love, and during their free time, they would often stroll together hand in hand. By the summer vacation, their passion had reached its peak, and they made a promise to be together forever. The girl had already obtained her family's consent, but Jin's father disapproved, hindering their relationship. The day before yesterday, Jin and the girl took a rickshaw to the Xiche Wharf. As it was still early before departure, they sat opposite each other in a small teahouse, chatting intimately. Before long, it was time, so they bought tickets and boarded the ship, transferring to Yangzhou. They stayed overnight. Yesterday morning, they took the first ship back to Zhenjiang. After boarding at Liuwei, they went to the cabin, still talking and laughing as usual. Unexpectedly, as soon as the ship started, they went out hand in hand to stroll around. When they reached the railing of the cabin in the middle of the journey, they embraced each other and jumped into the river. The ship stopped to search, but there was no trace of them. Only Jin's straw hat was hooked with a bamboo pole. When the ship arrived at the Zhenjiang port, the news spread throughout the city.

Decision on Local Expenses for Various Counties 105

The Jiangsu Provincial Government, in order to investigate the local budgets of various counties for the 22nd year, had already organized a Local Budget Committee to review them in advance according to the resolutions of the Provincial Committee. Due to the large number of documents and the need for detailed calculations, the review has not yet been completed. The current fiscal year has already begun, and all local undertakings in various counties cannot be suspended due to the undetermined expenses. Therefore, the Provincial Government Committee decided that the Review Committee should be urged to expedite the review. Before the review is completed, the counties are temporarily allowed to spend at 80% of the amount listed in the original draft budgets they submitted. Except for cases that have not been approved, the levies to be collected should still be collected according to the established cases. After the budget is finalized, it will be handled according to the budget. The Provincial Government has already ordered the counties to comply with this.

Investigation of the Case of the Jiangyin Provincial Committee's Complaint Against the Party Committee 106

Chen Xiping, a standing committee member of the County Party Headquarters Executive Committee, and Huang Bingying, an alternate member and general affairs officer, mutually accused each other of fraud and perjury. The Wuxi Court held a trial on the 31st of last month. Huang Bingying suddenly went to the Party Headquarters to retrieve a mirror frame for oaths and compared the seals with Chen Xiping. Chen Xiping called County Magistrate Ruan via long-distance telephone in Wuxi and had Huang arrested and detained. Huang refused to accept the detention and filed an appeal. He also presented a statement to the Provincial Party Headquarters, requesting relief. Yesterday (the 7th), the Provincial Party Headquarters sent Xiong Yufang (from Guizhou), an officer from the Civil Training Department, to Cheng to investigate. In the afternoon, he went to the County Party Headquarters and summoned Shen Qinru, a staff member who witnessed Huang Bingying entering to retrieve the mirror frame on the evening of the 30th, as well as the servant Qian Laosi and the guard Yan Bingrong, to inquire about the situation at the time. The Provincial Committee suspected Huang of taking more than 80 case files, as it was unlikely that so many cases could have been accumulated in one week. If the completed case files were to be archived, Committee Member Chen Lan should be responsible for checking them and determining which case files were missing. The reporter went to the Provincial Committee's residence at the Jiangyin Hotel and asked for his opinion after the investigation. Xiong stated that he was unwilling to say much before reporting back to the Provincial Executive Committee. He added that Huang Bingying's procedure for retrieving the mirror frame for oaths as an alternate member was indeed illegal. From the Party's standpoint, he should be subject to Party discipline, but the matter was suddenly handed over to the judiciary without reporting to the Provincial Government, which was somewhat inappropriate. It is reported that the Provincial Committee will stay in Cheng for one day and then return to the province to report.

Building Barracks and Requisitioning Private Land 107

The Ministry of Military Affairs had previously decided to expand the old Wangfu military camp near the Jiangyin district fortress to build a battalion of artillery barracks. An engineering office, the Jiangyin Works Office, was established to carry out the construction. The Property Clearing Office was also assigned to investigate its sketches and plans, and reported to the Ministry of Interior for approval and issuance of a public notice, which was posted by the Works Office. It is now scheduled to be convened by the Wang Works Office at 2:00 PM on the 10th, and all households concerned have been notified to elect representatives from each requisitioned mu to attend the meeting and participate in the discussion.

Eight Families in Baitaxiang, Yangzhou, Robbed by Bandits 108

Commissioner Ma, the administrative supervisor of the Ninth District, reported from Jiangpu County that eight families in Baitaxiang, including Hu Xingjiang, Li Xiangyuan, Qian Changfa, Zhao Chuanqing, Ding Yesong, Fang Qiyuan, Xu Zhaohua, and Hu Junyi, were robbed by seven or eight bandits in the middle of the night. The bandits, armed with homemade guns, knives, and clubs, continuously searched and robbed their homes, and stabbed the victim Hu Junyi. A large number of clothes, quilts, and farm tools were stolen from the victims' homes. The suspected bandit Ye Yunfang and some of the stolen clothes and quilts have been apprehended. The Commissioner has been requested to order his subordinates to assist in the arrest. Yesterday (the 8th), he specifically ordered the six counties under his jurisdiction, including Jianggao, to comply with the arrest.

Bandits Rob and Injure People in Qimingxiang, Gaoyou 109

The home of Wu Wenzhang, the head of Qimingxiang in the Seventh District of the county, was suddenly attacked by a gang of more than 30 bandits the night before. Armed with guns, they broke into the house and tied up Wu and his two wives with ropes, hanging them from the beams. They then burned their armpits with fire for half an hour, causing serious injuries. The bandits then rushed into the bedroom and conducted a thorough search, stealing more than 500 yuan in silver dollars before fleeing, firing their guns.

Qingpu Experimental Township Government to Be Established 110

The county government's plan to establish experimental township governments in various districts to promote autonomy has been submitted to the County Administrative Conference for discussion. Director Yao of the Twelfth District has drafted a plan and submitted it to the county government for filing. After repeated discussions at the district director's conference and the political affairs conference, a unanimous decision was made to proceed with the plan. After the township elections are completed, the district directors will select suitable locations and report them to the county for approval. It is reported that the districts have submitted their selected locations, and the township governments will be established separately soon.

Kidnapper Huang Suimao Captured in Ningbo 111

The kidnapper Huang Suimao, together with Shan Jiayuan, Shan Hanzhang, and others, kidnapped Zhou Songlin, a resident of Langjiaping near Wendongxi in Cidong last month, extorting a ransom of 700 yuan. They then tore up the ransom ticket and killed Zhou Songlin. Yesterday (the 7th) at 6:30 AM, the bandit was captured by detective Shen Shuangyu at Lingqiao Gate. Under interrogation, he admitted to kidnapping and extortion but claimed that the tearing up of the ticket was done by his accomplice Shan Jiayuan, and he did not know where the body was disposed of.

Fire in Jiangdong 112

Yin Wanxing's scrap cloth shop in Yangliu Street, Jiangdong, Ningbo, caught fire accidentally at around 1:00 AM on the 8th, suddenly erupting in flames. Fire brigades from various places rushed to the scene and worked hard to extinguish the fire. It took half an hour to put out the fire. A total of fifteen houses belonging to nine families, including Xu Maofeng's porcelain shop, Yu Shengxiang's shoe shop, Xin Xie Sen's stack, and the residences of Lu Jufang, Xu Ruisheng, Chuan Baoren, and Zhou Hantang, were burned down, with losses amounting to more than 10,000 yuan.

Female Employee of Hangzhou Municipal Government Commits Suicide 113

Ms. Zhang Xueqin, a 32-year-old staff member of the Health Department of the Hangzhou Municipal Government from Qingtian, graduated from the special class of the Provincial Medical and Pharmaceutical School. In the 16th year of the Republic, she served as a secretary of the Provincial Party Provisional Executive Committee and later joined the Health Department as a staff member. Zhang was known for her social skills and had many male friends. Her husband, Shen Kuang, from Xiaoshan, is currently working at the Statistics Council of the Ministry of Railways in Nanjing. Zhang and her seven-year-old son lived together at No. 7 Guangfu Road. On the morning of the 9th, she requested leave from the Municipal Government to go home because she was feeling unwell and went to bed. She did not wake up by the evening, and the maid went to call her, finding Zhang's face pale and barely alive. A whole bottle of sleeping pills was left on the bedside. Knowing that she had taken poison, the woman living with her, surnamed Zhu, immediately called a doctor for emergency treatment. At around 8:00 PM, she hired a car to take her to the Municipal Hospital for treatment, where she was given more than 20 injections of stimulants. By 4:00 PM yesterday (the 10th), she had not regained consciousness and was still in a coma. According to the doctor, she was able to drink a little orange juice and watermelon juice, and the period of critical danger had passed. Her husband was urgently telegraphed to come to Hangzhou to handle the matter. It is reported that Zhang had a violent personality, and her son was born from a previous marriage. After divorcing, she remarried Shen. For the past ten days or so, she had been going to the Wulinmen Highway Terminal every afternoon at 5:00 PM to wait for her male friend Lang Rongsan, but she had not met him. Her suicide is believed to be related to this.

Bandits Rob Yaojiawan in the Fourth District 114

Yesterday morning (the 4th), as soon as the village gate opened in Yaojiawan, the Fourth District, five or sixty bandits rushed in. The residents were still sound asleep and unprepared, and the entire village was robbed. Eleven men and women, including members of the Yao family, were kidnapped, and twelve rifles were seized. After being rescued by the militia from Sanheji and other places, the bandits fled southeast.

Water Police Team to Suppress Sea Bandits 115

The sea bandit Yan Zhenling's gang has been looting on the waters off Shengshan. Zhang Xianyi, the commander of the Fourth District of the Tongshui Police, has been ordered by Chairman Jiang via telegram to lead his teams, gather in Wusong, and set off to suppress the bandits.

Change of County Magistrate in Fengyang, Bengbu 116

Yuan Xingzhou, the county magistrate of Fengyang, was recently dismissed and investigated by order of the Provincial Government. His vacancy has been filled by Yi Jihe, who has been appointed to take over. Yi set off from the province after receiving the order and arrived in Fengyang on the 7th to take office in the coming days.

Investigating the Comfort-the-Army Donations 117

After the September 18th Incident, various circles in this area donated more than a thousand yuan in cash for the purpose of comforting the Ma troops. Unexpectedly, the funds were embezzled by the handler. The Investigation Committee of the Chamber of Commerce has repeatedly questioned the handler, who has ignored them. The Chamber of Commerce has decided to publish a warning and request that all circles unite to strictly pursue the matter in order to safeguard public funds and warn against evildoers.

▲Letter Correcting

To the Editor:

I am writing to correct a news item published in your newspaper on the 5th of this month regarding the incident of salt police assaulting people in Lujiahui, Nanhui, leading to a market strike. The facts described are not in accordance with the truth. On July 29th, the tax police stationed in Lujiahui seized more than 200 catties of contraband salt at a tailor shop in the town. Xu Yiqun (also known as Xu Fuzhao), who is known for protecting smugglers, gathered a crowd to obstruct the seizure and incite opposition to the sale of government salt. They then destroyed the government salt distribution office in the town, assaulting the shop clerks, and instigated the local security corps to chase and fire at the tax police. At the same time, they incited merchants and residents to strike in order to drive away the tax police and abolish the government salt depot. Fortunately, the officers and soldiers of the tax police exercised restraint and avoided a major incident. Subsequently, Jin, the director of the Nanhui County Public Security Bureau, Wang, the inspector, and Zuo, the patrol officer of Hangtou, together with Chen, the district director of the First District of our bureau, persuaded the merchants and residents not to be fooled. By the evening of the 30th, order had been restored. Unexpectedly, Xu Yiqun fabricated facts and falsely accused the tax police, confusing the public. The incident is related to the reputation of the tax police of our bureau. In addition to clarifying the facts and reporting them, we have specially written this letter to correct the situation and request that it be published in the letters column to clarify the truth.

Sincerely,

General Affairs Section, Songjiang Salt Affairs Tax Police Bureau

August 9th
