Fortunately, they were only slightly injured, so they were bandaged and discharged from the hospital.

Xu Bolin Drowns While Swimming After Returning from Work in Hot Weather 158

Xu Shigen from Yixing lives at No. 10, Lane 4, Lao Gongfang, Tanziwan, Zhabei. Xu has a son named Bolin, 24 years old, who works at the Dafeng Yarn Factory. At around 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, Bolin finished work and returned home. Because the weather was hot and stuffy, he went to the nearby Pengpu River alone to take a cold bath. Unexpectedly, because his swimming skills were not good, he sank to the bottom of the river and did not resurface for a long time, resulting in a tragic drowning. After being discovered, people urgently reported to his father, Shigen, who immediately hired workers to salvage the body. It took a long time to find it, but he had already been dead for a long time. Shigen was overwhelmed with grief. He reported to the Fourth District General Office. After a police officer investigated, he ordered the head of the district to report to the local court for an examination. However, the father of the deceased requested that the examination be waived.

Shandong Bandit Ma Hongfu and Gang Arrested 159

Escaped from Prison and Fled to Shanghai, Districts Ordered to Assist in the Arrest

The Cunning Rabbit Burrows Thrice, Two Women Deny It

The Municipal Public Security Bureau of this port recently received a secret telegram from the Tai'an County Government in Shandong, stating that Ma Hongfu, a notorious bandit chieftain from Shandong, had no fewer than several thousand followers and had been rampaging in various counties and villages in Shandong, robbing, burning, killing, and kidnapping for ransom. He had committed no fewer than dozens of major cases. Many of his followers had been arrested by various counties. Last spring, Ma was arrested by Tai'an County and imprisoned. Unexpectedly, within a few months, Ma led prisoners in the prison to take advantage of an opportunity to escape from prison. There were dozens of them in total. Since then, Ma has been at large and has been strictly wanted without success. Now, according to a secret report, Ma and his gang are hiding in Caojiadu, Shanghai. Please arrest them immediately, etc. Director Wen of the bureau ordered District Chief Tan of the Sixth District to investigate the matter quickly. District Chief Tan ordered Patrol Officers Gu Shao and Wei to conduct an investigation. After a week of investigation, they discovered on the night before last that Ma had three residences: Singapore Road, Connaught Road, and Jinsitu Temple. They immediately led more than ten officers, disguised, to secretly go to these addresses. They arrested two women at the three locations, one surnamed Ding and one surnamed Zhang (said to be Ma's wives or concubines, but both firmly denied it). They also arrested more than twenty suspects, including Mi Yingming, Yu Xinghan, and Mi Hongjun, and brought them to the district for interrogation.

Handgun Hidden in Lotus Root Starch 160

Several Criminals Arrested

Yang Xiguang, a Chinese detective of the Jiading Road Police Station, saw Jiangbei resident Yin Rufeng carrying a bamboo basket on Huade Road the day before yesterday. His appearance was suspicious, so he went forward to search him. Yin abandoned the basket and tried to escape, but was caught. Two packages were found in the basket. Upon opening them, they were lotus root starch. Inside was a handgun, loaded with five bullets. Accomplices Wang Shouxun, Liu Bukuan, Jing Yuhuai, Zhang Zhizhao, Gong Zhaofang, and a woman, Qian Qiushi, all from Jiangbei, were also arrested at No. 569 Yulin Road. Fifteen bullets were seized. All were taken to the police station and transferred to the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the case, requesting a postponement. After questioning the defendants, the judge ordered them to be detained for further investigation and interrogation at a later date.

Two Young Girls Lured and Raped by Rogues 161

Yin Hua, the 15-year-old daughter of Yin Xushi, a woman from Jiading, who resides at No. 196 Ximen Lane, Ximen Road, French Concession, went out shopping on the afternoon of the 6th of this month at 2:30 PM with Jiang Peiying, a 17-year-old girl from No. 59 in the same lane. Lu Zhengde, 26 years old, from Zhenjiang, who resides at No. 4 Yumin Lane, Route Prusse, and works in office No. 10 of the Jianghai Customs, and his friend Cai Lianbi, 23 years old, from this county, saw them and went forward to strike up a conversation. The two girls, because they were young and ignorant, were actually seduced and went to a movie theater to watch a movie. Later, they went to the Carde Hotel at No. 8 Fuxu Lane, Route Carde, in the British Concession and opened rooms No. 36 and 37. Lu Zhengde raped Yin Hua, and Cai Lianbi raped Xue Peiying. They separated at 11:00 AM the next morning. When Yin Hua returned home, her mother discovered the truth and wanted to investigate, but had no clue, so she temporarily endured it, waiting for an opportunity. Unexpectedly, Cai Lianbi missed his lover and went to Ximen Road to look for her the day before. Yin Xushi found out and reported it to the police, who ordered Detective Wang Yantian to arrest Cai and bring him to the police station. Yesterday, he was sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. The police lawyer Chen first explained the case, and said that the defendant had committed the crimes of Articles 257 and 240 of the Criminal Law, and asked for a postponement to supplement the arrest of his accomplice, Lu Zhengde, for joint investigation. Judge Li ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody for a continued hearing at a later date.

Red Pill Distribution Operation Cracked Down in Cigarette Shop 162

Red Pill King "Little Shandong" was previously arrested by the French police and released on bail by the Second Special Court and escaped. Last month, Zhang was arrested by the police and brought to court for trial. American Cotton and Wheat Arrives in Shanghai

China Merchants Bureau Obtains Storage Rights 164

Our country has purchased cotton and wheat from the United States. The first large batch of cotton can be loaded this month on the 15th and arrive in Shanghai on October 1st. This newspaper has already reported on this. Here is a follow-up report:

The cotton and wheat will be shipped to Shanghai in eighty ships, divided into batches. The cotton will be carried by ships chartered by the American merchant Fulai Foreign Company in this port, using forty ships to transport it in succession. The first batch of more than 7,000 bales will be loaded by the company's Aishan Aaron and will leave the United States on the 15th of this month. Because it has to stop at San Francisco, Japan, and other places, it will arrive in port around October 1st. The remaining 220,000 bales of American cotton will be loaded within three months, and most of it will be unloaded in Shanghai. The American wheat, totaling about 250,000 to 300,000 tons, will be carried by about forty ships chartered by the Norway-Weillmore Olsen Shipping Company and will also be delivered in Shanghai.

Central Government Not Responsible for Storage 165

Yesterday, a reporter learned from someone familiar with the cotton and wheat loan incident that the cotton and wheat purchased by the Central Government from the United States this time is different from the wheat obtained from the first loan, which was distributed by the Water Disaster Relief Committee. This time, when the cotton and wheat arrive in China, there will already be sales merchants responsible for the sale. The Central Government will absolutely not be responsible for storage and other responsibilities. After the cotton and wheat arrive in Shanghai, they will be handed over to the sales merchants in batches, and the designated storage location. The unloading process is completed. The merchants will handle the subsequent delivery of goods. The Ministry of Finance does not want to ask about it.

China Merchants Obtains Storage Rights 166

This time, the large quantities of cotton and wheat must all be unloaded in Shanghai. Each warehouse is vying for the right to store it. As a result, the China Merchants Steamship Bureau obtained the storage rights for the large quantity of cotton and wheat. The bureau believes that the ships carrying the cotton and wheat to China are at least 8,000 to 9,000 tons, and among the five docks in the bureau, the Huazhan Warehouse in Pudong is the most suitable, with the largest warehouse capacity and docks that can accommodate giant ships. After Liu Hongsheng contacted the Ministry of Finance's Cotton and Wheat Shipping Department about storage matters, an agreement has been reached. The bureau will provide two large docks for storage. The first batch to arrive will all be unloaded at the Huazhan dock.

Expediting Repairs to the Yangtze Warehouse for Use 167

Since the Yangtze Dock was taken over by the China Merchants Bureau, its advantages in terms of ship docking, unloading, cargo storage, and transportation are even better than those of the Huazhan Warehouse in the bureau. Taking advantage of the large number of American cotton and wheat arriving in Shanghai, the bureau decided to allocate funds for repairs in order to store the cotton and wheat. Yesterday, Liu Hongsheng proposed a resolution to the board of directors to allocate funds for the repair of the dock to receive and store the cotton and wheat. It is said that it has been approved. The original proposal is recorded below: Estimated cost of repairing the Yangtze Dock for public resolution. Proposed by Liu Hongsheng, Standing Director and General Manager. The Yangtze Dock has been taken over by the bureau, but it is in a state of disrepair. Whether it is rented out or used for the bureau's own business, it must be repaired before it can be used. It is estimated that the necessary repairs to the dock will cost approximately 47,000 yuan. After the project is completed, if the bureau operates it itself, it can undertake storage after American cotton and wheat arrive in China. Compared to the conditions of the Huazhan, the net profit can offset the repair cost in a little over a year. If the American cotton and wheat are actively shipped out, the net profit will be enough to offset the cost in half a year. Please make a public resolution.

Expansion of Labor Slowdown at British-American Tobacco Factories 169

Representatives of the Capital Side Request an Extension

Affecting the Entire Factory, Rendering Work Impossible

The labor slowdown in the leaf sorting section of the British-American Tobacco Company in Pudong continued yesterday without resolution. Mediation was originally scheduled for yesterday morning, but the representatives of the capital side suddenly requested a change. The labor unrest is about to expand, and other sections have been affected. Details are recorded below:

Continued Mediation Fails. The Social Bureau continued the mediation from the afternoon before yesterday at 10 a.m. yesterday. The representatives of the capital side, including Mr. Li De Ke (Director of the Personnel Department) and translator Chen Cangzhou, and the representatives of the labor side, including Chen Peide and Liu Dehua, were present, with Wang Gang of the Social Bureau presiding. However, the representatives of the capital side suddenly proposed to the chairman that they could not represent the factory at the mediation today and would submit a formal written statement explaining the reasons before attending again. Wang Gang immediately announced that the mediation would be temporarily suspended today.

Slowdown Affects the Entire Factory. The leaf sorting section continued its slowdown yesterday, and the entire section was shut down. By the afternoon, other sections such as gluing and box making were gradually reducing work due to the impact of the leaf sorting section shutdown. However, the factory's attitude turned tough. During the mediation the day before yesterday, the factory had agreed to reinstate worker No. 146, whose dismissal had triggered the slowdown, but refused to pay wages for the day of the slowdown, resulting in no resolution. Yesterday, the factory refused to mediate.

The pay-on-delivery system for political telegrams between China and the United States, which was originally scheduled to be discontinued on August 1, will resume on the 11th for all political telegrams transmitted wirelessly to and from the United States, according to news from the International Telegraph Office in Shanghai. Fifteen-Year-Old Girl Hangs Herself 172

Peeping into Neighbor's Bedroom and Uttering Indecent Words

Beaten Severely by Her Mother, She Commits Suicide in Anger

Kong Shen, a Ningbo woman residing at No. 70, Yongji Lane, Xihua De Road, had a daughter named Wenyin, who was fifteen years old. A few days ago, she peeped into the bedroom of a tenant living in the same house and uttered indecent words. After the tenant told the girl's mother, the mother was extremely angry and beat the girl severely. After being beaten, the girl was resentful and conceived the idea of ending her life. She secretly returned to her bedroom, took a rope, and hanged herself on the wall. Her mother caught sight of it and was extremely shocked. She immediately tried to untie her daughter, but she was already barely breathing and unable to speak. She rushed to report to the Huizhong Police Station, who ordered detective Chen Baozhong to investigate. The girl was taken by car to Shanghai Nursing Hospital, but she died on the afternoon of the previous day. The detective then transported the body to the Felton Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday morning, Zhang Junqing, the prosecutor appointed by the First Special District Local Court, arrived at the office to examine the body. After confirming the body, he took a public case and questioned the girl's mother, Kong Shen, about the previous situation. Zhang Jun then declared that the deceased girl, Kong Wenyin, had indeed died by hanging herself before death. The body was handed over to her mother, Kong Shen, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial.

Apprentice Dies in an Accident 173

Electrocuted While Repairing a Light Switch

Fan Zhongxing, a seventeen-year-old from Chongming, worked as an apprentice at the cigarette shop owned by Xu Zhonglin at No. 672, Annam Road. At around 2 p.m. the day before yesterday, a customer came to the store to buy a soapbox. The shop owner told the apprentice to go home immediately and fetch it, as the boxes were stored at his home at No. 57 on the same road. Unexpectedly, when he arrived at the owner's home, he found that the boxes were stored in the kitchen. Although it was daytime, the kitchen was very dark. The apprentice wanted to turn on a light to find the box, but the light switch was broken and could not be turned on. The apprentice then took off the switch to repair it himself, but he accidentally touched a wire and immediately fell to the ground, unconscious. Someone saw him and reported it to the Jing'an Temple Police Station, who ordered a detective to investigate. They then took him to the Red Cross Hospital, but the treatment was ineffective and he died soon after. The body was transported to the Felton Road Coroner's Office. Yesterday morning, a report was filed with the First Special District Local Court, and Prosecutor Zhang Junqing was appointed to examine the body. After confirming the body, he took a public case and questioned Xu Zhonglin and the deceased's father, Fan Waiming. Zhang Jun then declared that Fan Zhongxing had indeed died of electrocution before death. The body was handed over to his father, Fan Shaoming, who signed a guarantee to take it back for burial.

County's Fifth District Implements Epidemic Prevention and Medical Treatment 175

Xing Zhigang, the chief of the Fifth District of Shanghai County, concerned that the recent weather has been arid and the sun is scorching, and that the heat is stifling, is deeply concerned that the public may be infected with infectious diseases and cause endless troubles. City News 176

▲ Domestic Candy Gradually Develops. The Xianghai Machine Sugar Factory in this city produces Fanle Flavored Candy, Toffee, Cream Candy, etc., which are the most commendable and famous candies among domestic products. Its materials are excellent, its manufacturing method is sophisticated, and its machinery and equipment are perfect. The resulting candy is not only of good quality and delicious, but also clean and hygienic, surpassing foreign candies. It has already sold well in various ports. Now that there is a complete factory that creates high-quality domestic candy products, which are cheap and of good quality, it should be warmly welcomed by the Chinese people. ▲ Huade Watch and Clock Business Develops. The Huade Watch and Clock and Glasses Head Office across from the Continental Commercial Plaza on Damalu has been doing very well since its opening on the 5th. Its repair of watches and clocks and the matching of glasses are particularly accurate. Those who visit and patronize are truly in a state of crowded doors.

Events 181

Municipal Social Bureau

Draft Rural Revitalization Plan (Continued)

1. It is appropriate to alleviate the poverty of the countryside. Farmers rely on cultivating land, but due to various reasons, their income cannot meet their expenses, and it is difficult to maintain a family livelihood. Those who have income that can offset expenses often lack agricultural operating capital, such as the purchase of fertilizers and seeds, and the use of draught animals. They are unable to afford them, so even if they have good farmland, they cannot obtain good harvests. The more the harvest decreases, the poorer the farmers become. Therefore, it is appropriate to provide relief first. Upon investigation, the Municipal Social Bureau has held poverty relief loans and agricultural loans for the poor in this city. Not only have the poor in the city benefited, but also farmers in 11 areas in the four rural areas have been able to turn around with loans. However, the amount that one person can borrow from this loan is extremely small and cannot be lent to the fullest extent. To alleviate the poverty of farmers is like pouring a cup of water on a cartload of firewood, which is of no avail. It is hoped that the municipal government can raise huge amounts of money, strive to expand the loans, and provide farmers with as much loans as possible, so that agricultural finance can be circulated, and the poverty of the countryside can be medically treated. 2. Suppression of high-interest loans: Rural economy is difficult, and farmers lack funds, so they have to borrow from wealthy households. The wealthy households deliberately raise their interest rates and exploit them heavily. Because farmers want to solve their immediate needs, they have to accept it painfully. There are four types of rural high-interest loans: money high-interest loans, livestock high-interest loans, land high-interest loans, and goods high-interest loans. As a result of the rampant high-interest loans in rural areas, the self-cultivating farmers lose their land due to debt repayment and become tenant farmers. Tenant farmers are unable to rent land due to debt repayment, and they become hired farmers. They change again to unemployment, starvation and cold, and take risks, disrupt society, and destroy the countryside. Therefore, the country should strictly suppress high-interest loaners. If the legal maximum interest rate is exceeded, the law should be strictly enforced. At the same time, the government should set up financial institutions to make funds flow smoothly. In this way, rural life can be stabilized, and rural revitalization can be expected. 3. Protecting agricultural products and raising prices: Regarding this point, regarding the feast of the national rural economy, the municipal government should be asked to suggest to the national government to quickly implement protective tariffs and impose heavy agricultural tax rates on foreign countries. At the same time, it is recommended that all domestic transportation agencies reduce agricultural transportation costs and eliminate taxes so that all provinces and cities can sell each other smoothly and without obstruction. Then, tangible and intangible means are sufficient to increase the price of agricultural products and increase farmers' income. In addition, the exemption of common donations and miscellaneous taxes to reduce the burden on farmers, and the reduction of tenant rents to increase income, are all important ways to relieve the countryside. (To be continued)

Educational News

Special Feature National Defense Education (3) 182

Lecture by Professor Zhang Qiyun of Central University

Recorded by Zi Tao

Lecture 3: National Defense Education in Primary and Secondary Schools

This lecture focuses on teaching methods, divided into four aspects: stories, models, drills, and village compacts. They are explained in order below.

(1) Stories: Primary and secondary schools are for children's education, while universities are for adult education. Teaching children should focus on concrete things that appeal to the senses, not abstract and profound theories. Children enjoy listening to stories or reading novels, finding them fascinating. Good novels always provide many examples and avoid being too abstruse, grouping similar things together and progressing gradually. However, within many concrete facts, there are still general principles that run through them. Therefore, national defense education in primary and secondary schools can use the story method to subtly influence students' basic concepts of national defense, achieving a natural and effective result. For example, when explaining the importance of tanks, it can be incorporated into the story of the Nenjiang Battle, which is included in the geography textbooks of the three northeastern provinces. Initially, General Ma Zhanshan used Nenjiang as the first line of defense and broke several sections of the Taonan-Ang'angxi railway bridge. Later, Japan negotiated with us on the grounds of creditor rights. The Japanese stated that the Japanese army would not take any military action other than protecting the repair of the bridge and demanded that our side withdraw fifteen li from the Jiangqiao Bridge. Our side, considering that the League of Nations General Assembly was scheduled to be held on November 16, did not worry about other matters and allowed them to repair the bridge. After the bridge was completed, Japanese tanks and heavy artillery crossed the river and suddenly attacked us. In addition, at this time, the soil in Northeast China was frozen, tight, and dry, which was very suitable for travel. Japanese tanks and heavy artillery galloped back and forth, making it impossible to resist. According to military experts, if China had tanks and airplanes in the Nenjiang Battle, the result would not have been like that. For example, when the history class discusses the European War, a passage from General Ludendorff of Germany can be inserted. He said, "If our army had adequate tanks for military use in 1918, things could have been different." He also said, "I deeply know the combat power of tanks, but the highest military authorities always turned a blind eye to it, which led to an irretrievable defeat." General Von Zwehl of Germany also said, "We were not defeated by General Foch's genius, but by tanks." The status of tanks on the battlefield can be seen in general here. It is difficult to determine which is more important, teaching materials or teaching methods. Some believe that teaching materials lose their inherent value when separated from teaching methods, while others believe that teaching methods can adapt to circumstances, but if there are no good teaching materials to enrich them, they will inevitably become empty. In short, neither can be neglected. Currently, most schools in our country use textbooks as teaching materials. How to choose national defense teaching materials requires a lot of research. In addition to textbooks, we must also compile various children's reading materials, using extremely simple and lively language to describe various facts about national defense, and adapt them to the level of students at all levels for extracurricular reading.

(2) Models: The models discussed here are in a broad sense, including handicrafts and drawings. Children often want to make things, so handicrafts must be included in the curriculum. All toys can be made by the students themselves to train their minds and talents. For example, what does a tank look like? It is a special type of car with an internal structure similar to that of a car. The outside of the car is covered with steel armor to avoid the danger of guns and bullets. The car itself is equipped with machine guns and artillery, making it a disguised armored car. The special feature is that the four wheels of the car are removed and replaced by two chain tracks, with each section of the hinge connected in sequence to form a chain. Therefore, the tank is also known as a chain car. The tank travels by means of chain tracks and can climb mountains and cross ridges without any obstacles, making it very formidable. Schools can find ways to make a model of this new type of weapon and then have students imitate it, so that students can observe it personally to satisfy their desire for knowledge. At the very least, photographs or drawings should be available so that students can get a clear impression. For example, regarding naval ports or fortress projects, the staggered arrangement of bamboo and wood layers can be used to roughly represent the scale and show the situation. This type of handwork can allow students to imagine the place, and its effect cannot be replaced by language and writing. Generally, good naval ports have strict gateways and are surrounded by overlapping mountains, making them easy to defend. Natural barriers protect them, and enemy ships cannot directly attack from the sea. Gun emplacements and docks are built inside and outside the port, so there is nothing to fear. Although naval ports are not important ports for merchant ships to enter and exit, they have transportation routes to the interior, making it easier to gather materials. The supply of food, fuel, and other supplies is more convenient. If the location is inconvenient for land transportation, the port's situation alone is not suitable. To explain the various conditions of a naval port, it is best to use a model of Qingdao Port to represent everything. Good achievements in drawings, handwork, and various airplane models and gas masks can be displayed in the school museum for people to visit, as an aid to imparting military knowledge. As the saying goes, "Seeing is believing." The use of movies as an educational tool can give students a deeper impression. For example, the naval action movie produced by the US military is very exquisite and can inspire the American people to value the navy. After watching this film, it is as if one is on the scene and suddenly understands. Filmmakers in our country should also learn from this idea and produce films related to national defense. Because they have educational value, military experts and educators should be consulted to make them perfect. For example, homework during holidays is a good opportunity to implement design teaching methods. Teachers set a goal and make a plan in advance and then have students execute it. Finally, they add criticism. The execution procedures can be divided into investigation, collection, travel, practice, lectures, and visits. In short, students should be allowed to be active on their own and gain solid knowledge from their own experiences.

(3) Drills: The examination system has recently been implemented. I think it is still possible to vigorously implement drills. Drills are a great tool for implementing national defense education, as evidenced by the Sokol movement in the Czech Republic. The Czech Republic is a rising country in continental Europe, and its people are full of vigor, vitality, and strong unity, which is especially praised. The Czech Republic was able to gain freedom because of the training of the Sokol movement. The Czech word "Sokol" means "eagle in the island," taking its agility. It was founded in 1862, and its purpose is to develop youth sports and build an independent spirit. Today, the Czech Republic has a population of 15 million, and the Sokol movement has more than 700,000 members. The arena is located outside Prague, the capital, and its equipment can accommodate 150,000 people. Its construction cost 1 million yuan, which was entirely raised by members. During the competition, 100,000 young men and women swarm into the arena, and its music is magnificent and its order is strict, which makes people feel infinitely emotional. Members living abroad, not to mention in Europe, even those far away in the Americas, travel thousands of miles to participate enthusiastically, willing to sacrifice time and money to uphold the glory of the country. Although this movement is a kind of competitive sport, its spiritual training is infinitely great. The so-called "lying on firewood and tasting gall" and "millions of people are of one mind" can eventually cultivate a healthy national character and break free from the shackles of Austria. Massaryk, the great man who founded the Czech Republic, was one of the members of the Sokol movement. The area of the Czech Republic is roughly equal to that of Hebei Province in China, and its population is less than half that of Hebei Province. If our country adopts the drill system, it can be based on the old prefectures or sub-prefectures as units, depending on the convenience of transportation. For example, in Switzerland in Europe, even the smallest village has shooting exercises and sports meets, and the form in which they are held is very solemn, and the competition is very fierce. This kind of spirit is worth emulating.

Revision of the Contents of the Contract for Printing Selected Fine Editions of the Siku Quanshu 188

▲The Ministry of Education Announces the Organizational Outline of the Editorial Committee for Compiling Catalogues of Unprinted Fine Editions of the Siku Quanshu: After the Ministry of Education sent Jiang Fucong, Director of the Preparatory Office of the Central Library, to sign a contract with the Commercial Press on June 17 this year to print selected fine editions of the Siku Quanshu, the Palace Museum stated that the Wenyuange edition of the Siku Quanshu belonged to the museum and that the Ministry of Education should obtain the museum's consent before printing. After negotiations, the printing contract was revised and jointly submitted to the Executive Yuan for record by the Palace Museum and the Ministry of Education. The revised contents are as follows: (1) The Ministry of Education prints the Wenyuange edition of the Siku Quanshu under the entrustment of the Palace Museum; (2) The copyright belongs to the Palace Museum; (3) The Commercial Press gives one-tenth of the printed copies to the Central Library, which is changed to giving them to the Palace Museum. In addition to the two copies stored in the museum, the rest will be handed over to the Ministry of Education for international cultural gifts or exchanges.

(Nanjing, 10th) On the 10th, the Ministry of Education announced the organizational regulations of the committee for compiling catalogues of rare and unprinted editions of the Siku Quanshu, consisting of six articles. The main points are: 1. The committee members are all appointed by the Ministry of Education from among catalogue experts across the country; 2. For committee members not in Peiping, written opinions will be solicited, and the discussion time will be limited to one month. After the opinions are compiled, the committee members in Peiping will hold a meeting to formulate the catalogue; 3. The committee members are honorary positions; 4. The compilation of the catalogue will be limited to two months, after which it will be dissolved; 5. The meeting will be convened by the Preparatory Office of the Central Library as designated by the Ministry of Education.

Regulations for Appointment and Dismissal of Teachers in Municipal Elementary Schools 189

▲Revised and Promulgated by the Municipal Bureau of Education

The Provisional Regulations for the Appointment and Dismissal of Teachers in Municipal Public Elementary Schools in this city have been revised and promulgated by the Municipal Bureau of Education in accordance with the regulations for elementary schools issued by the Ministry. The regulations are recorded below: Article 1: The appointment and resignation of teachers in municipal elementary schools shall be temporarily handled in accordance with these regulations before the regulations for the appointment of teachers in elementary schools issued by the Ministry are promulgated. Article 2: Teachers in municipal elementary schools shall be qualified if they have noble character, adhere to Party principles, and are registered and qualified by the Bureau of Education. The registration regulations will be determined separately. Article 3: Teachers in municipal elementary schools shall be appointed by the principals from among the personnel registered and qualified by the Bureau of Education and shall be immediately reported to the Bureau of Education for record. However, if the Bureau of Education deems them unqualified, it may order a re-appointment. When reporting, the registration certificate issued by the Bureau of Education must be submitted for verification. Article 4: The term of appointment for teachers in municipal elementary schools is divided into three terms: the first term is one year, the second term is two years, and the third term is three years. After the third term, each term shall be three years. Article 5: Teachers in municipal elementary schools shall not be replaced without cause during their term of appointment. However, if any of the items listed in Article 91 of the elementary school regulations are found to be true after investigation by the Bureau of Education, their position may be terminated. Article 6: Teachers in municipal elementary schools are divided into graded teachers, specialized teachers, and assistant teachers. The rules for their treatment and service will be determined separately. Article 7: These regulations shall be implemented from the date of notarization.

梵恩斯业業餘資格

發生問題 205

Problems Arise

美草地網球會在審查中

American Lawn Tennis Association Investigating

因流言謂梵將成職業家

Due to Rumors that 梵 Will Become a Professional

(New York dispatch) Carl Seawright, chairman of the amateur rules committee of the American Lawn Tennis Association, announced today that the amateur status of American tennis champion 梵恩斯 is under review due to widespread rumors that he has dealings with the professional world. Upon hearing this news, 梵恩斯 said that this was a good thing, as it would clarify the rumors, but he only received a confirmed sum of remuneration.

Later, there was no further contact.

Recently, there have been rumors that 梵 plans to turn professional after the outdoor season and travel with Tilden. In fact, unofficial reports say 梵 has agreed to accept $100,000 for a nine-month professional contract, but this has never been confirmed. When asked, Oberlin, a key figure in the newly formed Oberlin Sports Promotion Company, admitted to negotiating with 梵恩斯. Oberlin also revealed that 梵 had requested $100,000 as a condition. Oberlin said that they were prepared to pay that amount, but 梵 must retain this year's U.S. Championship, otherwise the amount would be reduced.

It is generally believed that 梵 was about to turn professional last fall, but the compensation was not enough, so it did not happen. However, 梵 revealed that he would agree if the compensation was substantial enough. Tilden's behind-the-scenes power, last year offered a reward of $20,000, but 梵, having just defeated Cochem, was full of vigor and did not accept.

The actual net income of Tilden and Cochem's joint tour is about $210,000. The company owner earned $118,000. Ten matches in eleven days yielded this amount. 疋頭

Investigation of the Woolen Fabric Industry · Feng 219

The market for woolen fabrics was dominated by Western clothing 30 to 40 years ago, and the volume of transactions was not significant. After the change of clothing styles in the first year of the Republic of China, although Western clothing was not fully adopted, the woolen fabric business grew rapidly. More and more people wore Western suits, and the market for woolen fabrics became increasingly prosperous, leading to the present situation. The silk and satin business has declined daily, and the number of woolen fabric stores has increased. The industry originally had two main groups: Western clothing and general woolen fabrics. The Western clothing group was mostly located in the Hongkou area of Shanghai, while the general woolen fabric stores were mostly located in the Qipan Street area. In the last three years, the sales of woolen fabrics have increased even more. In cities, towns, and villages, all silk and satin and foreign goods stores now sell woolen fabrics. Most of the larger ones have set up separate woolen fabric sections. There are approximately 1,600 woolen fabric and Western clothing stores in Shanghai, both large and small. There are over one hundred formal stores that exclusively sell woolen fabrics (excluding those with established brand names). Therefore, it has become necessary to have a formal trade association, which is the Shanghai Woolen Fabric Trade Association. The following is a list of 75 member stores after investigation:

Cotton Flowers: August Contracts Rise on Short Squeeze 221

Silk, Tea, Silk Cocoon Market Roundup 223

(Good Autumn Silkworm Crop in the Four Townships North of Hangzhou) This year's autumn silkworm crop in the four townships north of Hangzhou is as good as the spring crop. The silkworms have developed well after hatching. During the second molt, the silkworms experienced some changes due to the weather, but the losses were minimal thanks to the efforts of the instructors. The silkworms are now in their third molt, and their condition is good. Barring any unexpected changes, a bountiful autumn cocoon harvest is expected.

(Sharp Fall in Lyon and Shanghai Factories) The Lyon raw silk market has been stagnant for a long time, and silk prices have been declining. According to reliable sources from French merchants, white silk prices in Lyon fell sharply the day before yesterday. Grade A silk was priced at only 97.5 French francs per kilogram, which translates to a decrease of more than 10 Shanghai silver dollars.

Grade B silk was priced at only 77.5 French francs, which translates to a decrease of more than 20 Shanghai silver dollars.

(Artificial Silk Sales Not Weak) Yesterday, the Yangtze River group continued to purchase 30 boxes of August and September futures contracts for brands such as Pai Da, Flying Eagle, and Blue Golden Bell at the exchange, with prices ranging from 174.25 to 163.75 yuan net.

(Foreign Firm Silk Grades Tend to Stagnate) The summer vacation for New York silk thread factories is nearing its end, and the factories are preparing to resume operations. However, silk inventories are substantial, enough to meet demand for more than a month. In addition, speculators are actively selling their holdings, so silk sales show no signs of recovery. Merchants in Shanghai are eager to sell, but European firms continue to suppress prices, and market sentiment remains sluggish. Yesterday, only Da Chang and others purchased 20 bales of white silk, and Xin Fu and others purchased 20 bales of Sichuan yellow silk. Prices remain flat and weak.

Needle Eyebrows Rise, Precious Eyebrows Fall 224

Yesterday, in the local foreign tea market, major foreign firms such as Ying Zhuang, Xie He, Yi He, Tong Fu, and Bao Chang continued to buy needle eyebrow green tea from Wuyuan and Tunxi. The market was especially strong for teas with tender, thin strips, which sold out as soon as they arrived. Sales prices rose by 3 to 4 yuan. However, the foreign firms showed little interest in precious eyebrow green tea, and prices for teas from Shexian and Suian have fallen below 100 yuan, a decrease of 4 to 5 yuan compared to before. The market conditions for other items such as pearl tea and tribute hee tea remained unchanged.

Grain Merchants Sell Distant-Dated Flour Futures 225

丨The decline is very sharp: exceeding three points丨

Yesterday, the flour market continued its downward trend. Although foreign wheat prices rose by 700-800 copper coins in Chicago and 300-400 copper coins in Canada, market sentiment remained weak. Spot flour sales were slow, and inventories continued to grow. Moreover, there was no longer any support from outside buyers. Manufacturers, recognizing the difficulty of reversing the trend, had to gradually unload their stocks. Buyers, seeing the opportunity, also gradually liquidated their positions. Therefore, the selling pressure was difficult to overcome. The near-month contract's decline stabilized somewhat as manufacturers covered their short positions (the lowest point reached was 2.225 yuan). The distant-dated contracts, however, fell more sharply as manufacturers sold short. Looking ahead, if sales do not improve, further declines are inevitable. As a result, the current month fell by 1 point compared to the previous day, September fell by

2.25 points, October fell by 2.5 points, November fell by 3 points, December fell by 3.25 points, and January fell by 3 points.

No Way Out for Flour, Wheat Prices Steadily Decline 226

Yesterday, wheat futures showed a declining trend. Foreign wheat prices had risen, and sentiment had temporarily stabilized. However, customers with goods in inland areas gradually sold short, and the market remained well-stocked. Manufacturers felt there was no way out for flour and were extremely lukewarm about buying wheat. This pressure was the main reason why the market could not hold its ground. Moreover, while the rise in foreign wheat prices could be temporarily dismissed, the wheat must eventually be replaced with Chinese wheat. The steady decline in prices for each month is therefore not surprising. As a result, the current month fell by 4 points compared to the previous day, September and October fell by 5 points, November fell by 6 points, December fell by 5 points, and January fell by 300 copper coins. Spot wheat, due to the lack of demand from manufacturers, was only being traded on a commission basis.

Free Talk

My Reply 231

— Ye Shengtao

丨Regarding the National Language Textbook丨

Today, I saw Mr. Yu Min's criticism of my "Kaiming National Language Textbook," and I would like to reply as follows:

Mr. Yu Min said that I wrote "馬托車" (mǎ tuō chē), and that according to the "national pronunciation," "people from all over the country will not understand what this is." In fact, there are many nouns with similar situations, such as "方棚" (fāng péng, awning) and "德律風" (dé lǜ fēng, telephone). As long as a person has heard of them, they will understand what they are. Moreover, haven't the words "馬達" (mǎ dá, motor) been almost "established" already? The "馬" (mǎ) in "馬達" (mǎ dá) is the same as the "馬" (mǎ) in "馬托" (mǎ tuō). However, I am willing to accept Mr. Yu Min's criticism and change the "馬" (mǎ) to "摩" (mó) to make it closer to the original sound.

The second point pointed out by Mr. Yu Min is actually his "accidental oversight." My poem begins with: "牆上開朶小紅花 (qiáng shàng kāi duǒ xiǎo hóng huā, A small red flower blooms on the wall). 牆下蝸牛去看花 (qiáng xià wō niú qù kàn huā, A snail goes to see the flower under the wall)." It ends with: "無數花開朶朶紅 (wú shù huā kāi duǒ duǒ hóng, Countless flowers bloom, each red), 一齊笑臉歡迎他 (yī qí xiào liǎn huān yíng tā, All smiling faces welcome him)."

Mr. Yu Min then said: "According to the grammar and habits of vernacular Chinese, it seems that '開朶' (kāi duǒ) means '開着一朶' (kāi zhe yī duǒ, blooming a flower); why does the following sentence change to '無數花' (wú shù huā, countless flowers)?" In fact, there are two sentences above the last two sentences: "爬爬歇歇三天半 (pá pá xiē xiē sān tiān bàn, Climbing and resting for three and a half days), 纔到牆頂看到花 (cái dào qiáng dǐng kàn dào huā, Only then did I reach the top of the wall and see the flower)." At first, only one flower bloomed, but after three and a half days, the flowers on top of the wall bloomed all over: this is exactly what I intended. Unexpectedly, it was overlooked by Mr. Yu Min.

"The Poor Man and the Rich Man" is an old fable. Because it contains the meaning of "people should conquer nature to make a living, and should not take the fruits of other people's labor," I chose it as teaching material, in connection with the previous lesson "Wind and Water." Mr. Yu Min took another view, believing that a lesson should be added after it, saying that the poor man "really went to farm, plow the land, chisel rocks, and cut trees, but landlords and others jumped out from the air, asking him to pay rent and settle accounts with him. He was deceived again. When he went to ask the rich man again, the rich man would tell him: 'I am cultivating my own land, who told you that you don't have land, etc.!'” This idea is very good. My thoughts took the path mentioned earlier, so I did not take this path. However, if the teacher is good at using it, I think even if it is not supplemented, it will not lead the readers astray.

××××××

A few days ago, there was also an article by Mr. Wu Dingdi, which made some suggestions regarding my words "Regarding the acceptance of literary styles, I advocate compatibility and extensive collection, and each article must be a model of each style." Now I will reply as an aside:

By literary styles, I mean basic styles such as description, narration, explanation, and argument. When we use language to express our emotions and ideas, we cannot do without these styles. How can a national language textbook not include these styles? By literary styles, I also mean the styles of practical documents such as notes, letters, telegrams, advertisements, articles of association, and opinions.

These styles are used daily and are encountered anytime, anywhere. How can a national language textbook not show some models

? I said "compatibility and extensive collection" earlier, but I did not specifically explain what I meant by the two words literary style, which caused Mr. Wu's suspicion; now that he sees this section, Mr. Wu should be relieved.

A Lawsuit about a Transformation Text 232

— He Ru

Recently, there was a lawsuit about a transformation text in the literary world that ended inconclusively. This interesting story should be told.

The plaintiff in this lawsuit was Wu Shichang. The sixth issue of the fourth volume of *New Moon* published Mr. Wu's critique of Zheng Zhenduo's illustrated *History of Chinese Literature*, which contained many criticisms, especially of the section on the origin of transformation texts, which was the most severely attacked. Mr. Zheng said:

We do not know when the earliest transformation texts occurred, but they must have been before the Kaiyuan and Tianbao eras. (Page 589)

As more and more Buddhist scriptures were translated, our writers and scholars were influenced by this new style and would imitate it unconsciously. (Page 588)

These are Mr. Zheng's views on the time and cause of the origin of transformation texts. Mr. Wu, on the other hand, believed that transformation texts originated from the Buddhist practice of singing and guiding. What is singing and guiding? The tenth chapter of Hui Jiao's *Biographies of Eminent Monks* states:

The purpose of singing and guiding is to proclaim the principles of the Dharma and guide the hearts of the masses. In the past, when Buddhism was first introduced, people gathered to recite the names of the Buddhas and perform rituals according to the scriptures. In the middle of the night, when they were tired and needed enlightenment, they would invite a virtuous elder to ascend the seat and preach the Dharma, sometimes interspersing it with accounts of causes and conditions or citing analogies.

It also says:

If one's knowledge is not broad enough and one's research is not deep enough, and one lacks the ability to improvise, then one must follow the old texts. However, if the talent is not one's own and the work is not one's own creation, then the pronunciation will inevitably be flawed. Moreover, any errors in transmission and writing will be followed and proclaimed, leading to confusion and doubt.

Mr. Wu's idea is that Buddhist preaching led to the practice of singing and guiding when the audience was tired in the middle of the night and needed enlightenment; that transformation texts arose from the interspersing of accounts of causes and conditions and the citing of analogies during the singing and guiding. According to *Biographies of Eminent Monks*, Hui Yuan was the leader, who lived from 333 AD to 416 AD, so the origin of singing and guiding was in the middle of the fourth century, and the text of the singing and guiding was the transformation text.

The defendant, Mr. Zheng, also presented a defense in a letter to Mr. Ye Gongchao, published in the seventh issue of the fourth volume of *New Moon*. Regarding the time of the origin of transformation texts, Mr. Zheng still insisted on his original view, believing that most of the transformation texts we see now are manuscripts from the late Tang Dynasty, and the earliest manuscripts with verifiable dates of authorship do not predate the Kaiyuan and Tianbao eras. Regarding the theory that transformation texts originated from singing and guiding, Mr. Zheng denied it outright, believing that singing and guiding texts were sung after meals, while transformation texts were not lectured after meals but in the main hall of Buddhist temples, and were not an epilogue. He also cited examples such as Emperor Jianwen of Liang's singing and guiding text and Wang Sengru's singing and guiding vow text selected in the fifteenth volume of *Guang Hongming Ji* as evidence, believing that these were singing and guiding texts, and therefore concluding that transformation texts and singing and guiding texts were two different things. It is unknown whether Mr. Wu was convinced after reading this article. In my humble opinion, it seems unlikely. The singing and guiding texts cited by Mr. Zheng seem to be texts for making vows and paying homage to the Buddha at the beginning of singing and guiding, not the singing and guiding text itself. As for the singing and guiding text itself, which sometimes intersperses accounts of causes and conditions and cites analogies, Mr. Wu's interpretation of analogies as stories may not be wrong. Moreover, Hui Jiao said:

At that time, the guide would hold a brazier and speak with eloquence and intonation, with endless arguments and limitless words. Talking about impermanence would make hearts and bodies tremble, talking about hell would cause fear and tears, asking about past causes would be like seeing past karma, verifying present results would be like showing future retribution, talking about happiness would make emotions joyful, and narrating sorrow would cause tears and grief. Thus, the whole assembly would listen attentively, the whole hall would be saddened, five bodies would be prostrate on the mat, heads would be broken in supplication, each would snap their fingers, and everyone would chant the name of the Buddha.

Reading this, we can imagine what kind of talent and attitude the guide must possess, what kind of materials must be used for singing and guiding, and what kind of effect singing and guiding can have on the audience. Are the singing and guiding texts cited by Mr. Zheng of this kind? Can they be of this kind?

I have no prior knowledge of either Mr. Zheng or Mr. Wu, and I have no bias in my opinion. Even in this lawsuit about a transformation text, I do not dare to assume the position of judge, but only offer my humble opinion for experts to correct. As for Mr. Wu's attitude in writing, he seems to be trampling on others, going beyond the scope of discussing academic principles. Although what he said may not be without pertinent points, it is obscured by his impoliteness. It is no wonder that Mr. Zheng was unwilling to engage in a point-by-point response and to devote all his energy to a brilliant defense, resulting in this lawsuit ending inconclusively. It is easy but not easy to be a critic.

"Soldiers" and "Bandits" 233

— Hu Chen

Third Grandpa patted the few dozen copper coins in his pocket and said loudly, "That's all that's left. The rest were taken away by those bastards!"

I just listened blankly, becoming interested in this old man who had fled from the neighboring village, and also feeling a little pity.

Third Grandpa slowly took a puff of his dry tobacco pipe, staring blankly at the white smoke that escaped from the corner of his mouth. After a while, he continued, "At first, they were just bandits, and we poor people weren't affected. Later, the soldiers came, using the name of chasing bandits as an excuse, and set a fire, even burning down our cowshed." He shook his head slightly, and finally sighed.

"On the evening of the eighth, everything was calm. The banditry of yesterday had also fallen behind the mountains with the sun. But in the middle of the night, we suddenly heard someone beating a gong and shouting 'robbers.' Later, we learned that it was the soldiers from the city who had come to suppress the bandits.

"The leader of the soldiers called himself a company commander. There were a total of twenty or thirty people, with more than ten guns. As soon as they arrived, they asked where the bandits had gone. When they heard that they had left yesterday, they settled down and stayed in the temple.

"The next morning, two people came and said that we had to send a load of rice every day and that each household had to donate half a dollar as military pay. He also said, 'This is your place, and we are protecting you, so this small obligation is something you should fulfill.' At that time, Shui Sheng interrupted with an irrelevant remark, and he was whipped a few times and tied up with hemp rope to the company headquarters. In the afternoon, all the soldiers came and said that they wanted to search for bandits in each house. They drove all the residents to the open ground, but they went inside and ransacked the houses. As a result, after the search, the more valuable things in the house went with them.

"Later, because they heard that there were bandits hiding in the village, they set fire to all the cowsheds, haystacks, empty houses, and so on.

"What's there to live for in our hometown? Planting a few acres of hard-earned land isn't even enough to pay the donations. He shook his head a few more times.

Looking at his wrinkled and withered face, I also shook my head. I couldn't help but think sadly: Where are the Chinese peasants going to make a living?

After Seeing "The Light of Motherhood" 234

— Autumn Wind

The long-awaited "The Light of Motherhood" has finally premiered at the Nanjing Grand Theater. I held high hopes for this film and rushed to the Nanjing Grand Theater, which was already packed, nearly sold out. This also proves that the gentlemen and ladies of Shanghai, like me, have high expectations for this film! Of course, there were also many who came without a specific purpose. After the newsreel, the main feature began. During the two hours of cinematic flow, it evoked my infinite sympathy and emotion.

Since the waves of love-supremacy and aestheticism spread to East Asia, many intellectual women who had just emerged from the darkness became intoxicated with aestheticism and sacrificed themselves under love-supremacy. Even now, it is unknown how many are still immersed in the maze of pursuing beauty! Love and beauty are only a corner of life and should not be allowed to dominate the entire life. "The Light of Motherhood" depicts a prisoner of aestheticism, a pitiful creature deluded by material pleasures. This tragic ending, thanks to the director's skill and the actors' efforts, can be said to be a rare gem among domestic films. Of course, it cannot be said that it is absolutely flawless, but I am not a film critic and dare not prattle. What I want to say here is a bit of sentiment after seeing "The Light of Motherhood."

The impression "The Light of Motherhood" gave me is: sadness and melancholy, and finding a way out in helplessness – divorce and starting a nursery.

The future is a world of storms. Either don't live in this world, or if you want to live in this world, how brave and strong should you be so as not to be enslaved by others? Indecision and blind longing are not paths to survival. I feel that the light in "The Light of Motherhood" is too weak. It only inspires us with tender maternal love and lacks courage and determination. Although in the end, the mother and daughter both escaped their caged family life to start a nursery, this can only be said to be a narrow path to survival found in desperation. Because the entire social organization is imperfect, relying on two or three poor people to initiate a nursery is actually very difficult. Therefore, the final ending of "The Light of Motherhood" makes us feel that they—the mother, daughter, and former father—are all purists, reclusive hermits, not warriors of the present world. They did not give us an inspiration of "strength."

"Such an amount is indeed their last hope, but I did not give them a reply on your behalf, and they also attached conditions."

Chapter Five (17)

Spring and Autumn

Scenic Areas Leaking to Automobiles 236

— Zhan Lu

The people of Suzhou have different psychological feelings towards automobiles driving in the city. Some are cold, cold to below freezing point, and some are hot, hot to above boiling point. The cold say: "There is only one and a half roads in the city where automobiles can drive; it is impossible to turn around and get out of the limelight. There is no benefit, but there are many harms. In the future, when city tigers run rampant, many lives will inevitably be sacrificed! The city is very peaceful, don't look for trouble." The hot say: "City areas should have the need to drive automobiles. It is necessary to demolish the surrounding city walls in the short term and open up all streets. Automobiles are sacred, and there is absolutely no reason to stop them."

The cold and hot arguments must be reconciled for a while. The method of reconciliation is to first allow automobiles to pass through scenic areas and then extend to cities. In this way, the scenery of Suzhou can attract tourists from all directions. Although it cannot compare to Hangzhou's West Lake, it can at least be close to West Lake's shoulder. The West Lake scenery is the elder brother, and our Suzhou scenery is the second brother.

It is embarrassing to say, "Above is heaven, below is Suzhou and Hangzhou." The Hangzhou scenic area has automobiles, and the Suzhou scenic area does not have automobiles. Hangzhou is indeed heaven, and Suzhou is no longer heaven. Every spring and autumn, our Suzhou people go to visit the West Lake scenery in an endless stream. As for our famous Taihu Lake Stone Lake, East and West Dongting, Guangfu Xuanmu, how many distant tourists can there be throughout the year? Not to mention distant people, even the people in the city circle who have visited these scenic spots are also a minority. Alas! It is in vain to be considered heaven, falling behind step by step, causing rural bankruptcy and creating such a gloomy paradise!

Suppose that "Qiufu" and "Fuhu" two automobile roads were built from Huqiu to Guangfu and Guangfu to Shihhu. Then, Suzhou's famous attractions and scenic areas can all be connected. Driving automobiles on those two roads, the wide areas can certainly reduce the danger of city tigers gnawing at people. The convenient transportation for tourists from all directions can attract at least tens of thousands of foreign tourists a year. People in nearby rural areas can engage in peddling and selling products. With more livelihoods, they can certainly revitalize the countryside, turning desolate areas into lively areas. All unemployed people can also make a living from it, without becoming bandits. It is truly called "one action and many benefits."

If you only add to the existing things in the city circle, let all the scenery be buried, and let all the rural areas decline. If all the wealthy people from the four surrounding towns gather in the city to sit in automobiles, eat big dishes, and watch movies, this is not a good phenomenon.

At the Movie Theater 237

— Ren Peichu

On Saturday night, I turned into the rooftop garden. I first strolled around each venue and felt that the Beijing Opera venue was too noisy, the storytelling venue was too quiet, the Qunfanghui was not to my taste, and I didn't understand the Dagudiao tune. I found the stairs, turned up, turned up, and turned into the open-air movie theater. This day, it was showing: Charlie Chaplin, Rock, Laurel and Hardy's "Comedy Mashup." Although they were all old films, I hadn't seen them, so I sat down.

The first film was Rock's "Scolding Neighbors." I laughed until my stomach hurt. Unfortunately, it was too short and ended in a moment. After it ended and was about to connect to the second film, the screen suddenly showed "Beware of Pickpockets." I touched my pocket and looked around. Just in that look, a beauty seemed to follow my gaze and came over and sat next to me. I looked at her in the faint light reflected from the screen and couldn't help but secretly comment, "Beautiful, fashionable, and sensual."

But I hadn't had a chance to make a move before she greeted me with a smile. Embarrassed, I quickly shifted my gaze to the screen: Charlie Chaplin was being slapped by a fat woman. Before I could react, she blew a thick puff of cigarette smoke out of her mouth and onto my face. Fortunately, I am also a veteran smoker, so of course I didn't need to dodge. Moreover, it was coming from the mouth of a beauty!

Eating with an Open Mouth 238

— A-Jie

The human body is not solid, so it has to eat and poop. Pooping doesn't require "art" and "method." This is a natural talent for people. There is no need to talk about it, just "urgently" poop. Only eating requires "art" and "method," not as easy as pooping. You see the deification of eating art and the wonder of methods in the world, which can prove that eating is not an easy task! For example, officials eat by bragging and flattering; shop assistants eat by jumping and leaping all day long, bragging about themselves; teachers eat by relying on a mouth in addition to chalk; friends who sing opera, sing civilized opera, and tell stories, of course, can't eat without a mouth. Except for rickshaw pullers who eat with their legs and prostitutes who eat with ×××, 90% rely on their mouths. Therefore, singing new operas and telling stories are commonly called "eating with an open mouth." In fact, most people in the world "eat with an open mouth," especially teachers.

In the past, how dignified were teachers? Heaven, earth, ruler, parents, and teacher sat in the fifth chair. Therefore, teachers received honorable titles such as "old master," "private tutor," and "master" without feeling ashamed. Today, whether they are university professors, lecturers, or teachers, a few gilded "Doctores" are accepted without shame. In fact, they are all "eating with an open mouth." What is so rare about it? In the common view, a gilded "Doctor" also holds a few teaching positions in universities and middle schools, carrying a briefcase, scurrying around all day long. He "barks" at X University, hurriedly runs to Y University, and "barks" again, then runs away. Often, the "lecture notes" become tattered, and the words in the book become so familiar that they flow out. However, the students' progress is small, but the teachers' progress is much greater. Isn't this very much like the masterpiece of "eating with an open mouth," with many performances?

At the same time, I got an invention. That is: "The tool for eating is the mouth, so the tool for eating is also the mouth." Why? Please do a statistic: Aren't those who are good at eating in the world all good at talking? Saying human words to humans, ghost words to ghosts, flattering words to those who are higher than me, boasting words to those who are lower than me, thickening the face, lifting the lips, drumming the long tongue, opening the talk box, with varying degrees of emphasis and intonation, subtly and forcibly, quickly and slowly, fluently and clumsily. The more artful the mouth, the greater the amount of food. Just look at the people who shake up in society, you might as well close your "conscience" but you can't close your "mouth." Isn't that a clear proof?

Those who do not understand "the art of life" are not the same. They are very clear in their hearts, but they do not speak out. People see him as a dumb, and they can't hear your honeyed flattery or your bragging skills, so they are unfathomable, and it is difficult to ask for advice. Alas! In the world, there is only "eating with an open mouth," and there is no "eating with a closed mouth." If you want to eat, quickly open your mouth!

I was pinched on the thigh, although it hurt, but I understood that this was a kind of flirting action!

She opened her mouth to me, asking me to sit in her house. This is a beauty favoring me! She stood up, seemingly anxiously waiting for me, but I, who did not appreciate the gesture, was still sitting still. She urged me several times and finally sat down again.

The surrounding electric lights shone brightly, and I realized that the movie was over. There was a burst of chaos between the seats. I disappeared into the chaotic crowd.

The Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 240

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Thirteen: Abandoning Duty to See a Soulmate, a Beauty Tacitly Agrees to Support the Family, What is Gained: A Strong Man Rejoices

Zhao Ziqiang said, "I've also thought about it. There are two ways out. One is to be a surgeon, and the other is to do business." Guan Yaowu was still standing, looking at him, and said, "Old brother, are you crazy? How can you say such a thing?" After speaking, he sat down. Zhao Ziqiang didn't say anything and took a sip of his wine. Guan Yaowu said, "Old brother, we've been soldiers all the way to now. We've been through a lot and changed three hundred and sixty bones. If you say there's some good thing that lasts forever, it's okay to give this up to do it. But it seems like you yourself are confident. I don't know whether it's being a doctor or being a shopkeeper. If you want to be a surgeon, you have to be a bit of a showman. We can't speak that way to people. And without someone to introduce and support you, you might not even be able to hang up the sign. Being a doctor is not like conscripting soldiers. You can't conscript people who aren't sick to come and see you. If people who are sick don't trust you, you can't conscript them to come and see you either. I have a friend who is very knowledgeable in medicine. He hung up a sign, got a certificate, and rented a house. He made a lot of noise. He waited at home for three months, and no patients came to his door. And he was an internist, not to mention a surgeon. If you say you want to do business, what kind of business do you want to do? No matter what kind of business, you always have to put up capital first. I want to ask you, how much capital can you put up?" These words left Zhao Ziqiang speechless. He drank his wine and ate his food, and after a long time, he responded, "Everyone has their own views." Guan Yaowu said, "How does everyone have their own views?" Zhao Ziqiang said, "For example, you have a wife and children, but you can't even go back for a whole day throughout the year. You have a home but it's like having no home:::" When Guan Yaowu heard him say this, he couldn't help but laugh out loud. He said, "I thought you had suffered some great shock and had to give up your gun! From the looks of it now, you're doing it to marry a wife." Zhao Ziqiang picked up his wine glass and took another sip, and then laughed, "It's not quite like that." (155)

Short Story

A Stream of Soothing 241

— Ms. Dingxiang

Closing the book and thinking quietly, the sorrows of the past and the discontented resentment float on my brow. I, on behalf of my sister who stood in the dark corner and wept, let out a stream of soothing.

Wasn’t it last year’s Lantern Festival when the child was born? As I came back from the cinema and walked through the courtyard, there was a courtyard of moonlight and swaying bamboo shadows. At this time, a few cries of a child came from upstairs. Oh! Concubine An gave birth. I went upstairs thinking.

Concubine An was wearing a sleeping cap, with a pillow under her head, her face pale, her eyes closed, lying on the bed. Gu Ma was sitting next to her with dull eyes. Where is the child? Wrapped in a cotton coat that Concubine An had worn before, lying at her mother's feet, crying hard with her eyes closed!

I said, "Concubine An! This is sinful. Whether the child is a boy or a girl, it is always your own. Today is the Lantern Festival, and a girl born on the Lantern Festival has a good life! Don't look down on her, let her warm up next to your body! Poor little life!" Gu Ma persuaded in a low voice. Concubine An still shook her head, and large tears fell from her eyes.

This child was really unfortunate. Concubine An eagerly hoped to have a son, so as to raise her status. But it happened to be a girl, which gave Concubine An a fatal blow. The child cried sadly! It seemed to understand her own life experience. Oh! Who is to blame? Blame this inherited society, right? The mother also sobbed on the pillow, as if sympathizing with the child, and saddened for herself.

The next morning, when I went to school, I didn't hear any crying. When I came back from school, I put down my schoolbag and looked for the child. In the corner of the house, on the floor, lay this unfortunate and sacrificed child.

This child was like a small flower on the green grass, quietly blooming in the spring breeze, and withering lonely in the spring breeze. No one knew, leaving only a stream of soothing.

In the Darkness 242

— Li Pengxiang

The farmer Li Xiaomao sat on the threshold of his thatched hut in the darkness, feeling dazed. He hated his wife for being too good at having children: this was already the sixth.

"What's the point of raising children in this kind of year? The output of the land is so worthless, more than two yuan for a load of barley. What will you give him to eat—drink northwest wind?"

As he thought angrily to himself, his son A-Da had already run out to tell his father that his mother had given birth to a younger sister.

So he followed his son into the room, where Granny Yin next door was bathing the newborn child in a footbath. The woman was groaning on the bed, and no one was taking care of her.

Suddenly, Li Xiaomao stiffened, took a few steps, pushed Granny Yin aside with one hand, and ran out with the footbath. The child was crying weakly inside, rolling around, but he didn't care at all. He put the footbath outside the room and went mindlessly to the stove to grab a bamboo basket of ashes, filling it to the brim. He took this back to the original place, gritted his teeth, lifted the bamboo basket, aimed it at the child's mouth and nose, and poured it in relentlessly. In a moment, there was no sound at all.

Granny Yin, who had been following him silently, was stunned. She looked at him inexplicably. Li Xiaomao's frightening expression scared her into immobility.

"What's wrong?"

She couldn't help but ask.

But he didn't answer, as if he hadn't heard. He poured the little thing into that bamboo basket. It didn't move at all, like a dead cat. So he took the bamboo basket, lit a lantern, carried the two things in both hands, ran out of the house, and walked away in the darkness along the narrow field path. Faintly, he could hear the barking of dogs in the village.
